# PLAN_ARCHIVE.md — Completed-milestone history

> Append-only companion to **[`docs/PLAN_SHORT.md`](PLAN_SHORT.md)**. PLAN_SHORT is the
> operational doc read at the start of every session, so it carries **only the current
> milestone**. When a milestone rolls, `/wrap-session` **moves** (never deletes —
> `docs/AGENTS.md` §4/§7) the just-closed milestone's completed-milestone section, its
> Decided entries, and its Done log into this file. **Newest archive batch on top;** within
> a batch the original reverse-chronological order is preserved verbatim. Nothing here is
> live — for open work and the current milestone see `docs/PLAN_SHORT.md`.

---

## Archived 2026-06-25 (Session 55): Milestone 4 — V1 polish

Moved out of `docs/PLAN_SHORT.md` at the **V1 → Public-readiness milestone roll** (`docs/AGENTS.md` §7; *move, not delete* — §4). Content is verbatim as it stood at the close of Session 54 (the M4 task section, every M4 Decided + Done entry, and the M4-resolved cross-cutting + Blocked items — plus the M2/M3-era resolved leftovers and the M2→M3 / M3→M4 curation-note blockquotes that had lingered inline). Newest batch on top; within each group the original reverse-chronological order is preserved.

---

**Completed-milestone task section (M4).**

## Completed milestone: Milestone 4 — V1 polish

_Retained as history — M4 ("V1 polish") is **feature-complete**: inline highlights, the entity side panel, manual correction in the reader (edit · merge/delete/undo · tag/un-tag/boundaries), and narrowed multi-story (per-story membership + the §3.4 this-story/whole-project scope toggle) all shipped and live-smoke-verified (Session 54). The world-graph parent was cut from PoC (S44). M4 completed all of V1 (the ingest→graph→viewer PoC, M0–M4)._

**Goal (spec §9 M4 / `docs/PLAN_LONG.md`):** the "V1 polish" set — **inline highlights**, side
panel, manual annotation, properties/relations edit, **multi-story**, ~~world-graph parent~~ — that turns
the working ingest→graph pipeline into a usable V1 authoring surface. **Scope narrowed 2026-06-22 (owner,
Decided S44): the world-graph parent (cross-story world merge, §3.6) is OUT of PoC → `docs/BACKLOG.md`;
multi-story narrows to "add a new story that reuses the project graph + per-story entity membership"
(no cross-story merge). The spec §3.6/§9 still describe the world graph — reconciling them is a pending
stop-and-amend before the multi-story slice.** Two seams M3 deferred **graduate
to live M4 work**: the **§3.4 graph story-vs-project scoping** (multi-story breaks the one-story-per-
project assumption the graph route rests on) and **DM-Rel-5**'s written-edge re-point (an
accepted-entity↔entity merge, first possible in M4, re-points an already-written edge). INV-2's
consent gate stays **deferred past M3** (persona-justified).

**First slice — M4.S1 inline highlights** (owner-chosen, 2026-06-17 roll). Decomposed step-0:
`architecture/proposals/m4-inline-highlights.md` (register **OPEN — DM-IH-1..8 / OQ-21**). A
**read-only projection** of the accepted graph (spec §3.5): render the story text, highlight accepted
entities inline (colour-by-type), hover→tooltip. **Centre of gravity = DM-IH-1 span resolution** —
`entity_mentions` carry **null char offsets**, so highlighting is a *where-does-this-entity-sit* problem
(render-time string search vs persisting real spans vs hybrid; PL inflection is the headline gap).
Side-panel, manual annotation, properties/relations edit, multi-story, ~~world graph~~ (cut S44) are **later** slices.

**Feature order** (sliced at the 2026-06-17 roll; later slices sequenced as decomposed):

1. **M4.S1 — inline highlights** (read-only reader + accepted-entity highlights + hover tooltip; spec §3.5).
   ✅ **DONE — backend (Session 32, PR #81) + frontend (Session 33, PR #86), live-verified.** Register
   resolved with the owner — DM-IH-1 (render-time search over name+aliases, *verify-first*: no stored
   span exists to persist), DM-IH-2 (new `GET /stories/{id}/reader`), DM-IH-3 (plain `<mark>` renderer,
   not Tiptap), DM-IH-4 (longest-match), DM-IH-7 (accepted-only), DM-IH-8 (name+type+aliases), DM-IH-5
   (reader-local fixed palette + hash fallback + legend, owner's call S33), DM-IH-6 (whole-story render;
   measured fine on the Oakhaven draft). Frontend = `features/text-reader/` (pure splitter + palette +
   `useReader` hook + `<mark>` renderer + tooltip + legend + route + graph link), test-first; both review
   passes ran. **Verified end-to-end by the Session-33 Oakhaven smoke test** (upload → chunk → extract →
   review/dedup → relations → reader), which surfaced ~12 post-PoC items now in `docs/BACKLOG.md`.
   _Next: side panel → manual annotation → properties/relations edit (incl. the DM-Rel-5 written-edge
   re-point) → multi-story + §3.4 scoping → ~~world graph~~ (cut S44). The smoke test argued for prioritising
   manual correction in the reader (it's where errors surface) — confirm slice order at resume._

2. **M4.S2 — entity side panel in the reader** (read-only inspection; spec §3.4 detail panel + §3.5
   "local graph around that entity"). **Owner-chosen 2026-06-18 (Session 34)** over manual-correction-
   in-reader — the read-only inspection surface the next slice's corrections build on. Decomposed
   step-0: `architecture/proposals/m4-side-panel.md` (register **DM-SP-1..8 resolved / OQ-22**). Click a
   highlighted entity → side panel with its details (canonical/aliases/type/**properties**/occurrences/
   relations/timeline) + a **1-hop [[ego-graph]]** mini-view. **Centre of gravity = DM-SP-1 data
   source → a focused per-entity endpoint** `GET /stories/{id}/entities/{eid}` (BFF: server-side
   cross-store join + the 1-hop neighbourhood + occurrences; needs a new `Neo4jRepo` 1-hop query),
   which **splits the slice** (DM-SP-7):
   - **M4.S2a — backend** ✅ **DONE (PR #89, 2026-06-18, Session 34).** `domain/neighbourhood.py`
     (pure `build_ego_graph`) + `Neo4jRepo.get_neighbourhood` (1-hop, project-scoped) +
     `GET /stories/{id}/entities/{eid}` (details + `properties` + ego-graph), test-first (8 unit + 5
     integration). Build-time refinement: occurrences are **not** in the endpoint — DM-SP-3 makes them
     the reader's rendered highlights, so S2b derives them client-side. `/code-review` folded one
     should-fix (project-scope the neighbourhood query).
   - **M4.S2b — frontend** ✅ **DONE (PR #91, 2026-06-18, Session 35).** `occurrences.ts` (pure,
     occurrences from rendered highlights) + `egoElements.ts` (pure, ego-bundle → cytoscape elements) +
     `useEntityDetail` hook + `ReaderEntityPanel` + `EgoGraphCanvas` + `ParagraphText`/`TextReader`
     wiring (click-to-open, neighbour navigation, occurrence drill → scroll + flash), test-first; 193
     frontend tests green. **DM-SP-4 resolved = cytoscape** (browser-verified live; neighbour-node
     inspection + drill-to-text both work). `/code-review` folded two findings (memoize `ParagraphText`;
     flash-timer cleanup). Read-only; editing is the next slice.
   Read-only this slice (INV-1/3/9 untouched); property/relation **editing**, manual tagging, "not this
   entity", and boundary changes are the **next** slice. _Then: manual annotation/correction →
   properties/relations edit (incl. DM-Rel-5 re-point) → multi-story + §3.4 scoping → ~~world graph~~ (cut S44)._

3. **M4.S3a — the side panel becomes editable** (the **first M4 *write* slice**; spec §3.4 "properties
   editable"/"relations editable" + §3.5 manual correction). Edit an accepted entity's
   `canonical_name`/`aliases`/`type`/`properties` + add/edit/remove relations between accepted entities.
   **Scope + decompose ✅ DONE (Session 36, 2026-06-19); register RESOLVED. Backend ✅ DONE (Session 37,
   PR #96); frontend ✅ DONE (Session 38, PR #98) — M4.S3a is COMPLETE.** "Manual
   correction in the reader" was sliced by **write-risk, lowest-first**: **S3a** (this) = edit existing
   entities + relations (no merge, no re-point, no spans); **S3b** = entity↔entity merge + DM-Rel-5/6
   re-point + whole-entity delete + undo-merge; **S3c** = manual tag/un-tag/boundaries (reopens DM-IH-1
   span storage); general split + relation temporal/source qualifiers = post-PoC (`docs/BACKLOG.md`).
   Step-0 → `architecture/proposals/m4-entity-editing.md` (`accepted`, register **DM-S3a-1..8 / OQ-23**
   resolved). **The first slice that *writes* committed graph state** — the design weight is the write
   path + reversibility, not the UI: **DM-S3a-1 = new named edit handlers + reword INV-9** ("exactly two
   writers" → "only human-reached handlers — accept, decide, edit"; ADR-0005 broaden-don't-mint
   precedent, **ADR drafted at build, test-first**); **DM-S3a-2 = a before→after edit-evidence log**
   (INV-3 undo + flywheel); **DM-S3a-3** route manual relation-adds through the existing decide path
   (sole edge-writer), re-predicate = delete+re-add, warn-on-MERGE-collision, allow self-loops;
   **DM-S3a-5** typed `properties` values (keys free, INV-4); **DM-S3a-7 = split** S3a-be / S3a-fe.
   - **M4.S3a-be — backend** ✅ **DONE (PR #96, 2026-06-19, Session 37).** `domain/entity_edits.py`
     (pure `apply_entity_edit`/`diff_entity`) + `Neo4jRepo.update_entity`/`delete_relation`/`get_relation`
     + `graph_edits` migration + `PostgresEditStore` + `EntityEditService` + `PATCH …/entities/{eid}` /
     `POST`+`DELETE …/relations`, test-first (396 backend tests green); OpenAPI snapshot + typed client
     regenerated. **INV-9 reworded + `docs/decisions/0006` (broaden-don't-mint)** landed; relation/
     candidate state-machine notes extended. **DM-S3a-3 resolved-at-build to a *direct* edge-writer**
     (option b): the decide path resolves endpoints by surface-name-within-a-paragraph, which a
     hand-picked edge lacks, so routing through it doesn't compose — owner-approved the pre-authorized
     fallback; INV-9's edge-writer set grows too. Both review gates ran (`/review-pr` caught a
     blank-predicate 500→422; `/code-review` caught a predicate whitespace-strip).
   - **M4.S3a-fe — frontend** ✅ **DONE (PR #98, 2026-06-20, Session 38).** `useEntityEdit`/`useAddRelation`/
     `useRemoveRelation` mutation hooks (+ `patchJsonBody`/204-safe `del` client helpers) with
     reader+graph+entity-detail invalidation (DM-S3a-4); a pure `propertiesEditor.ts` (typed scalar rows,
     nested/array values preserved as read-only JSON — DM-S3a-5/INV-4); `ReaderEntityPanel` gained an Edit
     mode (name/type/aliases/properties) + a relations add (reusing `EntityPicker`)/remove section with the
     `merged_into_existing` warning. **One small read-side backend add** (the lone deviation from "no backend
     change"): `language` on `EntityDetailResponse`, so the single name field writes the project-language
     `canonical_name_{pl,en}` slot — **bilingual-per-project is out of PoC scope** (spec §10 q8, owner). Both
     review gates ran; live-smoke-verified. Live smoke surfaced a UX nit (relation-direction toggle), folded.
   _Then: **S3b** merge/delete/undo (DM-Rel-5 re-point) → S3c tag/boundaries/spans → multi-story + §3.4
   scoping → ~~world graph~~ (cut S44)._

4. **M4.S3b — graph mutations that need downstream cleanup (merge · delete · undo).** The slice S3a named
   at its seam, and the **first to re-point already-written graph state**. **Scope + decompose ✅ DONE
   (Session 39, 2026-06-20); register RESOLVED.** Step-0 → `architecture/proposals/m4-s3b-graph-mutations.md`
   (`accepted`, register **DM-S3b-1..8 / OQ-25** resolved). Owner calls: **general undo** (any edit/merge/
   delete reversible newest-first via a grouped append-only `graph_edits` log — a *compensating transaction*;
   resolves spec §10 q2) **+ undo must *show what it reverses*** (each operation carries a human-readable
   description; preview + confirm); **merge = author picks survivor, resolves property conflicts by hand**
   (owner chose more control over survivor-wins); **real `DETACH DELETE` + full-snapshot undo** (not soft).
   INV-3 goes from *substrate* (S3a recorded) to *executed* (undo); INV-9 enumeration unchanged (ops live in
   `EntityEditService`); **split be/fe taken — and the be1(merge)/be2(delete+undo) cut taken too** (owner-
   chosen, Session 40); **ADR 0007** at build. **Spec amended (Session 39):** §3.4 (merge + delete in the
   detail panel) + §10 q2 (undo).
   - **M4.S3b-be1 — backend (merge)** ✅ **DONE (PR #102, 2026-06-20, Session 40).** The first operation to
     re-point already-committed identity: merge B into survivor A — pure `domain/entity_merge.py`
     (`plan_merge`/`detect_property_conflicts`: alias union, by-hand conflict resolution, content-addressed
     edge repoint/fold/self-loop) → `graph_edits` **grouping migration** (`operation_id`/`seq`/`op_kind`/
     `description`/`project_id`/`undone_at`) + `PostgresEditStore.record_operation` → `Neo4jRepo.delete_entity`
     + `repoint_entity_mentions` (RETURNING moved ids) → `EntityEditService.merge_entities` (**B deleted last
     so a crashed merge stays retryable** — the `/code-review` fold) → `POST …/entities/{eid}/merge`
     (400/404/409/503; OpenAPI + client regen). **ADR 0007** landed (merge/delete/undo contract + grouped-log-
     as-undo-substrate + write order); INV-9 grep guard widened (+`delete_entity`, fourth-instance); INV-3
     grouped-log note (substrate now, executed in be2); relation/candidate lifecycle notes extended. Both
     review gates ran; `/review-pr` folded two (incident-edge dedup, resolved-properties restriction),
     `/code-review` folded the write-order retryability fix. 427 backend tests green.
   - **M4.S3b-be2 — backend (delete + undo)** ✅ **DONE (PR #105, 2026-06-20, Session 42).** Whole-entity
     **delete** (real `DETACH DELETE` + full-snapshot before-image) + the general **undo executor**
     (`POST …/graph-edits/undo`, undo-last, preview + confirm): `PostgresEditStore.latest_live_operation`
     (COALESCE `operation_id`→`id`) / `mark_operation_undone` read path → pure `domain/graph_undo.invert_operation`
     → `EntityEditService.delete_entity` + `undo_last` (drift-check → 409, reverse-`seq` replay) → the two
     endpoints. INV-3 *executed*; `state-machines/graph-operation.md` (`applied → undone`) drawn; INV-9 fifth
     witnessed instance (undo reverses via the same human-reached writers). **Re-do-after-undo id collision
     resolved = a generation discriminator** (a `uuid5` seed suffix past any *undone* op for the same targets;
     retry-stable because a *live* op probes False) — kept the `undone_at` stamp model rather than the ADR's
     delete-the-rows alternative; applies to re-merge *and* re-delete. **DM-S3b-5 confirmed (owner, S42): allow
     the delete + let the merge's undo drift-check refuse** (no survivor-guard on delete). Both review gates ran;
     **`/code-review` caught a real data-loss bug** (`fold_relation` undo deleted A's pre-existing edge) — folded
     + two sibling undo-correctness fixes (folded-add no-op, remove-relation full-fidelity). Undo/delete
     **robustness hardening** (depth cap, single-`created_at`-per-op, neighbour-churn signal, row-factory dedup)
     → `docs/BACKLOG.md`.
   - **M4.S3b-fe — frontend** ✅ **DONE (PR #107, 2026-06-22, Session 43) — M4.S3b COMPLETE.** Reader/side-
     panel UI over the three merged routes, test-first (pure mapper → hook → component): `mergeConflicts.ts`
     (client-side conflict detection mirroring `detect_property_conflicts` — the merge 400 carries only key
     names, no values, so the by-hand resolver computes conflicts from both entities' `properties`);
     `useMergeEntities`/`useDeleteEntity`/`useUndo` (undo invalidates only on a *real* apply, not a preview);
     `MergeControls` (EntityPicker → conflict resolver → confirm → summary counts; self-merge blocked);
     delete-with-confirm in `ReaderEntityPanel`; `UndoButton` in the reader header (undo is *story*-scoped —
     owner call) with preview→confirm→apply + 404/409 handling. Both review gates clean; self-review nits
     folded (shared `formatPropertyValue`, reset-summary-on-pick, full-width merge section). **Browser smoke
     surfaced a backend bug → PR #108** (merge-undo 500); merge/delete/undo verified live after that fix.
   _Then: **S3c** tag/un-tag/change-boundaries (next — see item 5) → narrowed multi-story (new story +
   project graph + per-story entity membership; §3.4 scoping). **World-graph multi-story dropped from PoC
   2026-06-22 → `docs/BACKLOG.md`** (see Decided S44)._

5. **M4.S3c — manual tag / un-tag / change-boundaries** (the **final** "manual correction in the reader"
   slice; spec §3.5). **Scope + decompose ✅ DONE (Session 44, 2026-06-22); register RESOLVED.** Owner chose
   it as the next slice to build (over the narrowed multi-story work). Step-0 →
   `architecture/proposals/m4-s3c-manual-tagging.md` (`accepted`, register **DM-S3c-1..9 / OQ-26** resolved).
   **Centre of gravity:** a rendered highlight is a render-time *search hit with no saved identity* (DM-IH-1),
   so a manual span (inflected form / pronoun / new entity) can't be re-found by search and un-tagging has no
   row to delete. **Owner resolutions:** **DM-S3c-1 = (B) overlay / "save only what you touch"** (keep
   render-time search for auto highlights; manual tags persist stored spans that overlay+win; a rejected
   highlight writes a suppression the resolver subtracts; change-boundaries materializes one occurrence —
   incremental, no backfill, DM-IH-1's properties preserved); **DM-S3c-2 = both attach-existing +
   create-new-entity** (a new human-reached graph writer — INV-9 grows); **DM-S3c-7 = adopt Tiptap now**
   (owner override of my native-selection lean — V2 §4 editing inherits it; `/add-dependency` at fe build);
   tag/un-tag/boundary ride the S3b `graph_edits` undo (DM-S3c-5); add `source`+`mention_id` to
   `ReaderHighlight` (DM-S3c-6); **split be/fe** (DM-S3c-8); **no §3.5 capability amendment** (S3a
   precedent) — storage model + INV-9 reword in **ADR 0008** at build, a small **§6.4 data-model note** via
   stop-and-amend if the migration needs it. Completeness sweep over mention CRUD + entity-from-tag
   **closes** (no slicing gap; general split + relation qualifiers stay post-PoC).
   - **M4.S3c-be — backend** ✅ **DONE (PR #111, 2026-06-22, Session 45).** `domain/highlights.reconcile_highlights`
     (pure `search ∪ manual − suppressions`, manual-wins-then-longest-match, suppressions subtracted
     post-overlay; `Highlight` gains `source`+`mention_id` — `resolve_highlights` unchanged) +
     `entity_mentions.source` & a `mention_suppressions` table (migration `d5971b7919ab`, **§6.4 amended** via
     stop-and-amend — no §3.5 change) + five `EntityEditService` ops (tag-existing/tag-new/suppress/retag/
     change-boundaries) + four new undo op-kinds with inverters **contract-tested from the writer's real rows**
     (PR-#108 discipline) + routes `POST …/paragraphs/{pid}/{tags,suppressions,boundaries}` + the reconciled
     reader, test-first (523 backend + 247 frontend tests green); OpenAPI snapshot + typed client regenerated.
     **ADR 0008** landed + INV-9 reconciled (invariants.md sixth instance). Build refinement (ADR 0008 §4):
     rejection ("not an entity"/"not this entity") is **uniformly a suppression** (resolver clears it
     post-overlay, even over a manual span) — one mechanism, one inverse. Both review gates ran; `/code-review`
     folded one cleanup (`_mention_id` helper — dedup the id formula). DM-S3c-2 (tag-new) confirmed at build:
     `tag_new_entity` reaches the existing `create_entity` writer from the tag endpoint (no new graph symbol).
   - **M4.S3c-fe — frontend.** Split into two sessions (owner-chosen at the S47 plan, sizing the engine
     swap apart from the correction UI):
     - **M4.S3c-fe1 — Tiptap read-only migration** ✅ **DONE (PR #115, 2026-06-22, Session 47).** Replaced the
       per-paragraph `<mark>` renderer with one read-only **Tiptap editor + ProseMirror decorations** at
       behavioural parity (colour-by-type, tooltip, click + Enter/Space → side panel, occurrence flash); no
       write paths. Pure test-first modules `readerDoc` (paragraphs → doc, `paragraphId` per node) +
       `decorations` (codepoint→UTF-16 offset conversion against the original text — the verify-at-build, with
       an astral test — + decoration attrs); `ReaderEditor` is the isolated ProseMirror mount (no unit test,
       mocked in `TextReader.test`, browser-smoke-verified). Removed `ParagraphText` + `segments`. Dep:
       `@tiptap/*==3.26.0` (newest 3.x clearing the §6.7 soak, OSV-clean). Both review gates folded; browser
       parity smoke passed (it caught the read-only `handleKeyDown` gotcha — see Decided).
     - **M4.S3c-fe2 — the correction UI** ✅ **DONE (PR #117, 2026-06-22, Session 48).** Built on the fe1
       editor: pure `selectionOffsets.ts` (UTF-16 selection → codepoint span, inverse of
       `codepointToUtf16`); the **right-click context menu** (`ReaderContextMenu` — tag-as-entity on a
       selection; not-this-entity / re-assign / not-an-entity / change-boundaries on a highlight); the
       **`ReaderCorrectionPopover`** (reuse `EntityPicker` for tag-existing/re-assign + a new-entity form,
       open-world type); the three **mutation hooks** (`useTagOccurrence`/`useSuppressOccurrence`/
       `useChangeBoundaries`) invalidating reader/detail/graph; `decorations` emit
       `data-source`/`data-mention-id`/`data-start`/`data-end` so a right-click addresses the exact
       occurrence; `ReaderEditor` gained the selection-capture adapter (PM selection primary, native DOM
       fallback — the lone untestable surface, browser-smoke-verified). Change-boundaries = **re-select +
       confirm** (owner-chosen UX). Undo reuses `UndoButton`. ADR 0008 §4: both rejections POST a
       *suppression*, never a delete. No backend/schema change. 285 frontend tests (+39); both review gates
       folded; owner browser smoke confirmed all flows. **"Manual correction in the reader" is now
       feature-complete (S3a edit · S3b merge/delete/undo · S3c tag/un-tag/boundaries).**
   _Then: narrowed multi-story (new story + project graph + per-story entity membership; needs its own
   decompose + a §3.6/§9 stop-and-amend) → V1 polish wrap._

6. **M4.S4 — multi-story** (add a new story that reuses the project's shared graph + per-story entity
   membership; spec §3.4 scope toggle / §3.6 narrowed model — the cross-story *world graph* is OUT of PoC,
   cut S44). Decomposed S50 (`architecture/proposals/m4-multi-story.md`, register **RESOLVED** DM-MS-1..7);
   the defining finding was that membership is **derivable** (no new storage) and the matcher seed is
   already project-scoped, so the slice is additive. Sliced opener → backend → frontend:
   - **M4.S4-opener — `world_id` cleanup** ✅ **DONE (PR #124, Session 51).** Drop the always-null
     `projects.world_id` column + plumbing across 6 homes + the §3.3 code-mirror reword (migration
     `c0c7904a555c`). The low-risk opener for the slice.
   - **M4.S4-be — backend** ✅ **DONE (PR #128, Session 52).** Story-scoped graph read
     (`scope=story|project`, **default `story`**, pure `domain/story_scope` filter + derived membership,
     null-source manual edges story-agnostic) + `project_id`-on-upload (404 on dangling project) +
     `GET /projects` (derived `story_count`) / `GET /projects/{id}/stories`; OpenAPI/typed-client regen.
     **No new migration, no new dependency.** `/code-review` folded one id-only-query efficiency fix.
   - **M4.S4-fe — frontend** ✅ **DONE (PR #130, Session 53).** `useProjects`/`useProjectStories` hooks; a
     `scope` param on `useStoryGraph`; the `ProjectPicker` at `/projects`; the §3.4 this-story/whole-project
     graph toggle; add-story-into-project (URL-carried context). Test-first; 306 frontend tests. `/code-review`
     caught 3 real bugs the self-review missed (reload-loses-context, missing cache invalidation,
     panel-blank-on-toggle) — all folded. Cross-story graph-cache coherence deferred → `docs/BACKLOG.md`.
   _Then: the live multi-story smoke (next session) → if clean, M4 is feature-complete → the M4→next-milestone roll._

---

**Milestone-4 Decided entries** (reverse-chronological, verbatim).

- **2026-06-24 — Session 54: M4 multi-story LIVE SMOKE = PASS → M4 feature-complete; dev-data workaround for a silently-truncated story; 10 graph-quality findings harvested (no production code).** The end-to-end verification of the shipped multi-story feature (S51+S52+S53). **Method:** stack already up; migrated the dev DB (it was behind at `d5971b7919ab` → head `c0c7904a555c`); drove the **API surface** (no browser-automation tool in this env) while the owner drove the browser UI. **Verified:** `GET /projects` picker data; **add-story-into-project** (oakhaven-2 → Oakhaven, `story_count` 1→2); **cross-story dedup** (oakhaven-2's candidates matched against oakhaven's accepted graph — 56 merge proposals → 24 distinct story-1 entities); the **§3.4 scope toggle** filtering both **nodes and edges** correctly (`scope=story` 88n/93e ⊂ `scope=project` 176n/228e, identical from either story) — owner confirmed the toggle live. **Workaround decision (dev data):** the auto-chunker had **silently truncated oakhaven-2** — its LLM outline dropped all of Chapter Six's content (kept only the header), so the reader showed 19 paragraphs and extraction never saw the storm/boarding scenes. Because the system has **no re-structure (409) and no delete-story** (both deferred features), and a full manual re-structure would orphan the already-confirmed entities' mention-links (breaking `scope=story` until a full re-extract+re-review), the owner chose to **preserve the confirmed work**: a targeted DB insert of the 6 missing Chapter-Six paragraphs (text pulled via the real `parse_manual_outline`, dry-run-verified, 6 `INSERT`s only — nothing deleted) + a **resume-extract** that processed *only* those 6 paragraphs (the per-paragraph checkpoint skipped the 19 done) → a small Ch6 candidate batch the owner reviewed. Result: complete story (25 paragraphs), all prior confirmations intact, Ch6 entities/relations in the graph. *Considered & rejected:* a clean manual re-structure (correct structure but loses all the review effort — the thing the owner explicitly wanted to keep); leaving it truncated (owner wanted the complete story). **Findings → `docs/BACKLOG.md` (10) + a cross-cutting spec-drift (1):** auto-chunk no-retry-on-overflow **and** the more serious **silent content-drop / no coverage check** (`manual` is the only trustworthy structuring mode until fixed); a "New entity" card with an armed (amber) merge target reads as if Accept will merge; merge candidates show only name+score (can't verify *which* entity — sharpened by the score-100 "crew" false-merge, two different ships' crews); the relation card shows **no source context** (can't commit a relation blindly); modality/irrealis, n-ary arity, and eventive-vs-stative + timeline-ordering as relation-modelling gaps; predicate proliferation (semantic relation merge); the graph view as a direct editing/curation surface; and the **spaCy PreNER spec drift** (§6 step 3 / §3 step 4 describe PreNER as an active pipeline stage, but it's dormant — the live `/extract` is LLM-only) → routed to cross-cutting as a stop-and-amend, with the spaCy-without-LLM eval captured in backlog. **Retro:** reflective pass run — nothing cleared the bar for a skill/rule change; owner concluded the session (skip `/retro`). **Roadmap direction DECIDED this session (owner):** M4 done = all of V1/PoC complete; the next-phase sequence is **Public-readiness/docs → Graph-quality polish → V2 Editing → V3 Style** (`docs/PLAN_LONG.md` amended — M2/M3/M4 ticked, the two new milestones inserted before V2). The **Public-readiness pass is next** (README + demo artifacts + code docs + the two spec↔reality reconciliations [PreNER dormant, world graph cut] + doc hygiene — lock the portfolio presentation before the next build); then a **Graph-quality milestone that opens with a backlog-triage conversation** (the 10 Session-54 findings) to make the graph trustworthy before writing features. **The mechanical roll execution** (byte-exact archive move of M4 → `PLAN_ARCHIVE.md` + scaffolding the Public-readiness task list) is the next session's first task — deferred from this long conversation, kept light. *Considered & rejected:* jumping straight to V2 (build writing on an untrustworthy graph); doing the graph-quality work first (a stranger should land on a legible repo before we polish internals). **Checks:** docs-only session (`docs/BACKLOG.md` + `docs/PLAN_SHORT.md` + `docs/PLAN_LONG.md`) — code gates n/a; the *running app* was the verification.
- **2026-06-24 — Session 53: M4 multi-story FRONTEND slice shipped (PR #130) + oakhaven-2 sample (PR #131).** Built the §3.4 reader/graph experience over the S52 backend, **test-first**, consuming the existing typed-client surface (no backend/generated-client change). **Owner scope call (resume):** include the **add-story-into-project** path, not a read-only picker+toggle — so multi-story is reachable and demonstrable end-to-end through the UI. *Considered & rejected:* read-only picker + toggle only (the scope toggle would have nothing to toggle without a UI way to put a 2nd story in a project). **Design choices:** (a) `useStoryGraph` carries `scope` as the **3rd query-key element** (`["story-graph", storyId, scope]`) so the existing 28 prefix-invalidation callers (`storyGraphQueryKey(storyId)`) still refetch both scopes and a flip repaints from cache — no caller churn (*rejected:* changing the shared key signature); (b) the add-to-project target rides the **URL** (`?project_id=&project_name=`), not router `location.state` — a `/code-review` finding (state evaporates on reload → silent new-project); (c) on upload success, **invalidate the project + project-stories caches** keyed off the response `project_id` (a `/code-review` finding — was stale 30 s); (d) the graph scope toggle **resets the node selection** (a `/code-review` finding — a node picked project-wide blanked the panel when narrowing). **The dual review gate paid off (the PR-#36 pattern again):** `/review-pr` (self) declared clean; `/code-review` (high, 8 finders) caught those **3 real bugs** + the 30 s-stale list + the panel blank — all folded with tests. **Deferred (owner-approved):** cross-story project-scope graph-cache coherence — a graph edit invalidates only the edited story's prefix, leaving a *sibling* story's project-scoped view stale for 30 s; self-healing, no data risk, the fix touches ~11 unrelated mutation hooks → `docs/BACKLOG.md`. **The oakhaven-2 sample** (a continuation of `oakhaven.md`, Chapters 4–5, with deliberate coreference cases) shipped as its own docs-only PR (#131), split out per "don't scope-creep". *Considered & rejected:* folding the sample into the FE PR (unrelated). **Checks:** 306 frontend tests green (was 285); build + lint clean; all 4 CI jobs green on both PRs; owner gave the per-merge OK on each.
- **2026-06-24 — Session 52: M4 multi-story BACKEND slice shipped (PR #128).** Built the resolved register (DM-MS-1..4) **test-first**, no new decompose: story-scoped graph read (`scope=story|project` on `GET /stories/{id}/graph`, **default `story`**) via a pure `domain/story_scope.filter_graph_to_story` fed by derived membership; optional `project_id` on upload (404 on a dangling project — fail-closed); `GET /projects` (+ derived `story_count`) and `GET /projects/{id}/stories`. **No new migration, no new dependency** (membership is *derived*, DM-MS-1). Shared `ErrorResponse` extracted to `api/responses.py`; OpenAPI snapshot + typed client regenerated. **Edge-rule refinement (owner call, this session):** a hand-added relation carries no `source_paragraph_id`, which the resolved DM-MS-2 rule didn't consider; owner chose **null-source edges are story-agnostic** — shown in `scope=story` whenever both endpoints are story-members. This preserves DM-MS-2's "`scope=story` is a no-op for single-story projects" guarantee (the literal rule would have hidden manual edges). *Considered & rejected:* applying the literal rule (would drop manual edges from single-story views). **Review:** `/review-pr` clean; `/code-review` (high, 8-angle) found no bugs and one efficiency fold — `scope=story` was loading 768-dim mention embeddings just for `entity_id`, so added a lean id-only `list_entity_ids_for_story` (commit `4966368`). 543 backend + 285 frontend tests green; all CI jobs green. Frontend picker + §3.4 toggle is the next slice (separate PR).

- **2026-06-23 — Session 50 (M4 narrowed multi-story step-0 decompose + register RESOLVED + a tiny spec amendment; design/planning only — no production code).** The next M4 slice's full design pass; "manual correction in the reader" (S3a/S3b/S3c) is feature-complete. Step-0 → `architecture/proposals/m4-multi-story.md` (`accepted`, register **RESOLVED** DM-MS-1..7 / OQ-27). **The defining finding: the narrowed slice needs almost no new machinery.** Reading the as-built (3 Explore sweeps) showed (1) **per-story membership is already derivable** — `entity_mentions.paragraph_id → paragraphs → scenes → chapters → stories.id` is a real FK chain and the rollup query already exists (`postgres_repo.py:437-458` `list_entity_mentions_for_story()`); (2) the **matcher seed is already project-scoped** (`accepted_entity_reader.load_accepted(project_id)`), so a new story in an existing project auto-matches the project's known entities with **no cascade change** (the §B.4 incrementality test); (3) the **reader is already multi-story-correct** (project-scoped entities + story-scoped mentions). So the genuine gaps are only: create-story-**into-an-existing-project** (today every upload mints a new project), project/story **list** endpoints (none exist), and a **story-scoped graph read** for the §3.4 toggle. **Owner resolutions (one plain-language question at a time):** **DM-MS-1 = DERIVE membership from `entity_mentions`** (no new storage; single source of truth; edge membership via `source_paragraph_id`'s story — *rejected* a Neo4j property/edge and a membership table); **DM-MS-2 = a `scope=story|project` param on the existing `GET /stories/{id}/graph` route, DEFAULT `story`** — the owner **refined my `project` default → `story`** (safe because for single-story projects the two scopes return the identical graph, so the default flip is a no-op until a project gains a 2nd story; edge rule (i): show an edge only when both endpoints are story-members ∧ its source paragraph ∈ the story; *rejected* a new `/projects/{id}/graph` + re-pointed route); **DM-MS-3 = optional `project_id` on `POST /stories/upload`** (omitted ⇒ new project as today; "same upload, pick project first"); **DM-MS-4 = add `GET /projects` + `GET /projects/{id}/stories`** (read-only; implicit project creation kept, explicit `POST /projects` deferred); **DM-MS-5 = the `world_id` cleanup rides this slice + amend §8.4/§3.3 "whole world" → "whole project"**; **DM-MS-6 = verified already covered by M4.S3b** (the merge re-points incident edges — DM-Rel-5; multi-story adds no new merge trigger, nothing to build); **DM-MS-7 = split be/fe, backend one slice, the `world_id` cleanup the low-risk opener.** **No new invariant, no state machine, no ADR** (the slice is additive — DM-MS-1 *removes* a would-be data boundary by deriving). New glossary term `[[multi-tenancy]]` (project = the *tenancy key*, stored; a story = a *derived sub-scope*). **Spec amended this session (DM-MS-5, owner-approved):** §8.4 toggle + the §3.3 handpick-scope cross-reference, "whole world" → "whole project" (the S49 world-graph-out sweep keyed on "world graph" and missed these "whole world" phrasings — the "homes hide behind different words" lesson again; grep-verified no "whole world" remains in the spec). **New backlog item (owner side-note):** *dual-store data architecture* — revisit whether the Postgres+Neo4j split is optimal at PoC→V2 (`docs/BACKLOG.md`, ties OQ-1). *Considered & rejected:* storing membership (a second source of truth to sync); changing the existing graph-route semantics (DM-MS-2 b — a behaviour change for no PoC gain). **Checks:** docs/vault/spec only — no code, no deps; code gates n/a. **Next: build test-first** — the pure membership-rollup property → `world_id` cleanup (the opener) → `project_id`-on-upload + list endpoints + story-scoped read → OpenAPI/typed-client regen → then the frontend slice (picker + §3.4 toggle).

- **2026-06-22 — Session 48 (M4.S3c-fe2 built + merged, PR #117): the reader's manual-correction UI — "manual correction in the reader" is now feature-complete.** The fe write surface on top of the fe1 Tiptap editor (spec §3.5). **(1) The selection verify-at-build passed; the offset math is a pure tested module.** `selectionOffsets.selectionToSpan` maps a paragraph-relative **UTF-16** selection → **codepoint** span (the inverse of fe1's `codepointToUtf16`, via a new `utf16ToCodepoint`), rejecting empty/reversed client-side so a guaranteed-400 is never POSTed; astral + round-trip tested. **(2) The `editable:false`-constrains-selection risk (the S47 heads-up) was handled by a two-path adapter.** `ReaderEditor` resolves a selection via ProseMirror `editor.state.selection` first (gives a paragraph-relative `parentOffset` directly) and falls back to the native DOM `Selection` (walking the paragraph's text nodes) — the lone untestable surface, isolated + mocked in the container test, **browser-smoke-verified** (the owner confirmed selection + right-click both work read-only). **(3) Change-boundaries UX = re-select + confirm (owner-chosen)** over drag-handles / numeric inputs: pick the action → a banner → drag the new span → Confirm; reuses the one selection pipeline, no custom ProseMirror widget. A search hit materializes (no `mention_id`), a manual span edits in place (`mention_id` set). **(4) A right-click addresses the exact occurrence via DOM data-attrs** — `decorations` now emit `data-source`/`data-mention-id`/`data-start`/`data-end` (codepoints), the same pattern `handleClick` already uses for `data-entity-id`; no text selection needed for a highlight correction. **(5) Both rejections POST a suppression, never a delete (ADR 0008 §4)** — pinned in the hook + container tests. **(6) The three hooks invalidate reader+graph+entity-detail unconditionally** (the S3a rhythm) — cheap, avoids branching on whether a new entity was minted. **No backend or schema change** (routes + typed client already on `main`). **Reviews:** `/review-pr` clean; `/code-review` (high) refuted two correctness candidates (`data-start/end` always co-emitted with `data-entity-id`; the `""`-paragraphId URL is never constructed because `mutate` only fires while a phase is set) and folded one efficiency finding (gate the mouseup selection-resolve to boundary mode). **Owner smoke** found steps 2/4 (tag/re-assign to an existing entity) *working-as-designed* — the tagged form surfaces in the panel's **Occurrences** timeline (derived from highlights), not in aliases (DM-S3c-1 rejected alias-only) — and raised two post-PoC UX items (type hints; surface manual forms as aliases/known-forms), both recorded in `docs/BACKLOG.md`. *Considered & rejected:* a shared hook factory + a reusable toggle control + typed DOM-attr contract (`/code-review` candidates) — speculative abstraction inconsistent with the existing `useEntityEdit`/`handleClick` patterns (Karpathy). **Checks:** frontend 285 pass + lint/format/build clean; no deps changed; CI green on all four jobs; browser smoke confirmed all flows; owner gave the per-merge OK. `/retro` skipped (owner — the reflective pass found the rituals + the S47 handoff served the session well, nothing cleared the bar).
- **2026-06-22 — Session 47 (M4.S3c-fe1 built + merged, PR #115): reader migrated to Tiptap read-only + ProseMirror decorations.** Session A of a two-session split of M4.S3c-fe. **(1) Split the fe slice into fe1 (engine swap) + fe2 (correction UI), owner-chosen at the plan.** The full fe slice (a new dep + a render-layer rewrite + selection→offset + a right-click menu + tag picker + new-entity form + 3 mutation hooks) was too big for one reviewable session; fe1 reaches *behavioural parity* on Tiptap and lands the risky engine swap on its own, fe2 layers the write UI on top. The completeness sweep over the four correction operations confirmed they all home in fe2 — no slicing gap. *Considered & rejected:* one session/PR for the whole fe slice (a large diff across the render layer + 3 write paths, and a long stretch before a check-in). **(2) The verify-at-build was an offset-unit mismatch, handled by a pure tested module.** The backend emits highlight offsets as Python **codepoint** indices; ProseMirror counts **UTF-16** code units — they diverge by one per preceding astral character. `decorations.codepointToUtf16` converts against the *original paragraph text* (the same care `domain/highlights.py` takes), unit-tested with an emoji case; the same primitive inverts for fe2's selection→offset, so proving it here de-risks fe2. **(3) Minimal Tiptap extension set, no StarterKit** (Document + a custom Paragraph carrying `paragraphId` + Text) — the read-only reader needs no editing marks/history; fewer deps to pin. **(4) One whole-story editor, not per-paragraph** (my call, stated in the plan) — idiomatic, performant (DM-IH-6 measured whole-story render fine), and it gives fe2 a clean position→(paragraph, offset) mapping through the document model rather than the rendered DOM. **(5) The read-only `handleKeyDown` gotcha (caught by the browser smoke):** ProseMirror's `handleKeyDown` is an *edit* handler PM only runs while the view is editable, so on a read-only (`editable: false`) editor it never fires — Enter/Space-to-activate-a-highlight must be a React/DOM handler (a wrapper `onKeyDown` reading the focused span's `data-entity-id`), not a PM plugin prop. Click worked throughout because `handleClick` is a *regular* handler. **This is a live heads-up for fe2: `editable: false` also constrains text *selection* on a ProseMirror view — fe2's core mechanism — so selection handling there must not assume the default editable-view behaviour.** **Reviews:** `/review-pr` flagged the keyboard parity + an empty-doc `setContent` guard; `/code-review` (high, multi-angle) confirmed **zero correctness bugs** in the offset math/reactive sync and surfaced the tooltip-fallback parity + a `Flash`/`ReaderFlash` type dup + coverage gaps — **all folded**. `ReaderEditor` is an isolated untestable mount (no unit test, mocked in `TextReader.test`, browser-smoke-verified) — the same boundary as the cytoscape canvases. *Considered:* threading the highlighted surface text into the tooltip fallback (folded, for exact parity with the prior `<mark>`). **Checks:** frontend 246 pass + lint/format/build clean; dep-age green (`@tiptap/*==3.26.0`, 17 days old at pin, OSV-clean); CI green on all four jobs; browser parity smoke passed; owner gave the per-merge OK. `/retro` skipped (owner — the reflective pass found the browser-smoke-catches-what-jsdom-can't convention already fired as designed).

The owner conditioned the doc fix on verification ("check we're sure they're present; are we using them or just here to be here?"). Traced the loop: written on accept (`candidate_review.py` → `entity_mentions.embedding`), loaded back per entity into the accepted snapshot (`list_mention_vectors_for_entities`), consumed as max-cosine in `MatchingAgent.stage2` — both the initial cascade and on-accept re-match (M3.S4c). - **2026-06-22 — Session 45 (M4.S3c-be built + merged, PR #111): manual tag / un-tag / change-boundaries — overlay storage.** The backend for "manual correction in the reader" (spec §3.5), the final write-risk slice (S3a edit · S3b merge/delete/undo · **S3c** tag/un-tag/boundaries). Built test-first against the resolved DM-S3c register. **(1) §6.4 stop-and-amend (owner-approved before the migration):** `entity_mentions` gained a **`source`** column (`'extraction'` default vs `'manual'` — an *explicit* flag, not a "non-null span" heuristic, so the two stay distinguishable if extraction ever stores offsets) + a new **`mention_suppressions`** table (`paragraph_id` FK+cascade; `entity_id` nullable, no FK — the OQ-1 cross-store seam). **No §3.5 capability amendment** (S3a precedent — §3.5 already specifies the corrections). The amendment also noted the pre-existing §6.4 sketch omits the M3 `entity_mentions.embedding` column — flagged as a follow-up (see Blocked/questions), *not* fixed here (unrelated drift). **(2) Build refinement recorded in ADR 0008 §4: rejection is *uniformly* a suppression.** "not an entity"/"not this entity" both write a `mention_suppressions` row the resolver subtracts post-overlay — *including over a manual span* — rather than deleting manual rows. One rejection mechanism, one inverse (`RemoveSuppression`); honours DM-S3c-1(B)'s "a rejected highlight writes a suppression record." This dropped a planned `delete_mention` forward op-kind. *Considered & rejected:* deleting manual rows on rejection (two code paths + two inverses for no user-visible gain). **(3) DM-S3c-2 confirmed at build:** `tag_new_entity` reaches the *existing* `create_entity` writer from the tag endpoint — INV-9's enumeration grows by a *path*, not a new graph-writing symbol (like the undo executor; the mention/suppression mutators write Postgres only, the staging side of INV-9's line). Recorded as INV-9's **sixth witnessed instance**. **(4) Reconciliation is a pure domain contract:** `reconcile_highlights = search ∪ manual − suppressions`, manual-wins-then-longest-match, suppressions post-overlay; `resolve_highlights` left unchanged (S1/S2 reader intact); `Highlight`/`ReaderHighlight` gain `source`+`mention_id` (DM-S3c-6). **(5) Undo rides the S3b grouped log** via new op-kinds (`add_mention`/`create_entity_from_tag`/`suppress_span`/`edit_mention_span`), inverters **contract-tested from the writer's real recorded rows** (the PR-#108 producer↔consumer discipline); tag-new/atomic-retag/materialize-boundary are grouped single-step-undo ops. **(6) ADR 0008** authored (owner-confirmed) + INV-9 reconciled across `invariants.md`/proposal banner/INDEX. **Reviews:** both gates ran — `/review-pr` clean (no blocking); `/code-review` found **zero correctness bugs** and folded one cleanup (`_mention_id` helper — the id formula was repeated 4×, a drift would silently break undo-by-id). **Retro:** reflective pass run; nothing cleared the bar for a new rule (the existing regenerate-isn't-reconcile guard + producer↔consumer discipline + two-gate review all fired correctly). **Checks:** backend 523 pass + ruff/`mypy --strict` clean; frontend 247 pass + lint/format/build clean; CI green on all four jobs; owner gave the per-merge OK.
- **2026-06-22 — Session 44 (scope decisions + M4.S3c step-0 decompose).** Mid-session owner scope calls, before any S3c code. **(1) WORLD-LEVEL multi-story is OUT of PoC → `docs/BACKLOG.md`.** The "world graph" — a story belongs to a shared *world X* whose entities become cross-story merge candidates (spec §3.6; the world-graph-parent M4 slice) — is **dropped from the PoC**. This reverses the prior "basic world-graph is in-PoC" framing (the backlog's *World graph from multiple sources* section, updated this session). **(2) The narrowed multi-story capability STAYS in PoC: add a new story that *reuses the existing project graph*, with a graph migration tracking *which entity appears in which story* (per-story entity membership — a property/label or a per-story container).** Purpose: scope the reader/graph to "this story vs the whole project", **and** let known entities **leverage extraction** in a new story (seed the matcher with the project's accepted entities). This **concretizes** the long-deferred **§3.4 story-vs-project scoping** cross-cutting item (the data-model mechanism behind its "this story / whole world" toggle) — it is the in-PoC direction, *not* the dropped world-graph. Owner framed it as "first thing we'll add" for the multi-story work. **(3) New post-PoC backlog item: code documentation generation** — first stone toward *living* project-code documentation (docs derived from source, kept in sync; design wide-open — recorded as a direction). **(4) Pending stop-and-amend (flagged, not yet done):** the spec still *describes* the world graph as in-scope (§3.6 + §9 M4 feature order); reconciling §3.6/§9 to decisions (1)+(2) is a **propose → owner-approve → amend** task before the multi-story slice is built (not a quiet edit). *Considered:* keeping world-graph in PoC "at basic level" (the prior note) — owner reversed it; the narrowed membership capability gives the useful half (per-story scoping + extraction leverage) without the cross-story-merge complexity. **(5) M4.S3c step-0 decompose ran AND its register was RESOLVED this session** (the session's main deliverable) → `architecture/proposals/m4-s3c-manual-tagging.md` (`accepted`, register **RESOLVED** DM-S3c-1..9 / OQ-26). The slice = the **final** "manual correction in the reader" slice (S3a · S3b · **S3c** tag/un-tag/change-boundaries; spec §3.5). **Centre of gravity:** today a rendered highlight is a render-time *search hit with no saved identity* (DM-IH-1; `entity_mentions` offsets are NULL/unused), so a manual span (an inflected form, a pronoun, a new entity) can't be re-found by search and un-tagging acts on a highlight with no row to delete. **Owner resolutions:** **DM-S3c-1 = (B) overlay / "save only what you touch"** — keep render-time search for auto highlights; a manual tag persists a **stored span** (real offsets) that overlays + wins; a rejected highlight writes a **suppression** the resolver subtracts; change-boundaries **materializes** that one occurrence — incremental, **no backfill**, DM-IH-1's rename-free/edit-robust properties preserved (*rejected:* (A) materialize-all = a migration + discards those properties; (C) alias-only = can't do change-boundaries or single-occurrence un-tag). **DM-S3c-2 = both attach-existing AND create-new-entity** (a new human-reached graph writer — INV-9 enumeration grows; needed to catch an entity extraction missed). **DM-S3c-3** occurrence-level (not-an-entity suppresses; not-this-entity suppresses + optional atomic re-tag); **DM-S3c-4** materialize-then-edit; **DM-S3c-5** tag/un-tag/boundary **ride the S3b `graph_edits` undo** (new op-kinds + inverters, contract-tested from writer output per the PR-#108 lesson); **DM-S3c-6** add `source`+`mention_id` to `ReaderHighlight`; **DM-S3c-7 = ADOPT TIPTAP NOW — owner override** of my native-selection lean (pay the editor setup so V2 §4 editing inherits a robust selection/decoration engine; Tiptap = a new fe dep → `/add-dependency` at the fe build; the `<mark>` renderer becomes Tiptap read-only + ProseMirror decorations); **DM-S3c-8** split be/fe; **DM-S3c-9 = no §3.5 *capability* amendment** (the S3a precedent — §3.5 already specifies manual tagging + the three corrections), storage model + INV-9 reword land in **ADR 0008** at build, with a small **§6.4 data-model note** (human-authored mentions carry real offsets) via stop-and-amend if the migration needs it. **Checks:** docs/vault only — no code, no deps.
- **2026-06-22 — Session 43 (M4.S3b-fe built + merged, PR #107; backend merge-undo bug fixed, PR #108) — M4.S3b COMPLETE.** The frontend for graph mutations, plus a bug its smoke surfaced. **(1) Undo affordance lives in the reader *header*, not the entity panel (owner call).** Undo is *story*-scoped (`POST …/graph-edits/undo` reverses the last edit *anywhere* in the story), so a per-entity placement would be semantically wrong. **(2) Property-conflict resolution is computed *client-side* from both entities' `properties`, not from the merge 400.** The merge route's 409/400 conflict body is a plain `{detail: string}` naming only the conflicting *keys* — no values — so a by-hand "pick which value to keep" resolver can't be driven from it; `mergeConflicts.buildConflictRows` mirrors the backend's pure `detect_property_conflicts` over both entities' fetched properties, and the 400 stays a safety net. *Considered & rejected:* round-trip the 400 then fetch values anyway (a wasted round-trip + a fragile string-parse). **(3) `useUndo` invalidates caches only on a *real* apply, never on a preview** (a preview touches nothing). **(4) The merge-undo 500 was op-name drift, fixed in PR #108 (split out, not scope-crept into the FE PR):** the merge writer records `op="discard_self_loop_relation"` (`_merge_rows`, `f"{kind}_relation"`) but `graph_undo.invert_operation` matched the bare `"discard_self_loop"`, so a self-loop-dropping merge's undo raised `UndoNotInvertible` → unhandled → 500 (delete-undo and self-loop-free merges were fine). CI stayed green because the inverter's unit test *hand-built* a fixture with the op name the writer never emits. **Fix:** match the real op + a **writer↔inverter contract test driven from real `_merge_rows` output** (closes the gap); the misleading fixture corrected to the real name (now a true regression). **No spec amendment** (ADR 0007 already covers the contract). **(5) Review-queue cross-cutting nits NOT discharged** — the S42 handoff optimistically said S3b-fe would discharge the "review-UX folds" note, but the reader-editing slices (S3a/S3b-fe) never touched the extraction/relation *review queues*, so the `CandidateView` merge-target-name / per-screen error-mapper / shared-`useReviewQueue` nits remain open (they fire only when a *review queue* next changes). **Retro:** two rules added — (a) `backend/src/story_forge/AGENTS.md`: test a string-coupled producer↔consumer contract from the producer's *real* output, not a hand-built fixture (the general form of the §2 fabricated-fixture lesson); (b) `frontend/AGENTS.md`: during a live smoke, use a `git worktree` for a parallel hotfix rather than `git checkout`-ing the working tree off the branch under test. **Checks:** 460 backend pass + ruff/`mypy --strict` clean; frontend build/lint/test green (247); CI green on both PRs; both review gates ran on #107; owner gave the per-merge OK on #108 and #107; merge/delete/undo verified live in the browser.
- **2026-06-20 — Session 42 (M4.S3b-be2 built + merged, PR #105): whole-entity delete + the general undo executor — INV-3 *executed*.** The first slice that *reverses* recorded graph operations. **(1) DM-S3b-5 survivor-delete confirmed (owner): allow + drift-refuse.** Deleting an entity that is an earlier merge's survivor is allowed unconditionally; if that merge's undo is later attempted, its drift-check refuses (409). No "is this a survivor?" guard on delete — the consistency check is pushed to undo, which already has a drift mechanism. *Considered & rejected:* block-the-delete (adds a survivor-lookup to every delete + a new failure mode for a window drift-refuse already covers). **(2) Re-do-after-undo id collision resolved = a generation discriminator** (the ADR 0007 design point). The deterministic `uuid5` operation id (keyed on the operation's targets, for crash-retry idempotency) collides if the *same* targets are re-operated after an undo recreates them. The build **kept the `undone_at` stamp model** and suffixes the seed with a generation = count of *undone* ops for those targets (`_op_seed`/`_next_generation`); a *live* op probes False so a retry re-derives the same id (idempotent), only an undone prior op bumps it. Applies to re-merge **and** re-delete. *Considered & rejected:* the ADR's delete-the-undone-rows alternative (discards the audit trail, contradicts the stamp model the be1 schema was built for). **(3) Layering:** pure `domain/graph_undo.invert_operation` (rows → ordered inverse plan + declarative drift check, reverse-`seq`) ; I/O in `EntityEditService.delete_entity`/`undo_last`; read path `PostgresEditStore.latest_live_operation` (COALESCE `operation_id`→`id` so S3a singletons are undoable — they now also carry `project_id`) / `mark_operation_undone`. INV-3 *executed* in `invariants.md`; INV-9 fifth witnessed instance (the undo executor *reverses* via the same human-reached writers — adds no new writer); `state-machines/graph-operation.md` (`applied → undone`) drawn. **(4) `/code-review` (multi-agent) caught a real data-loss bug `/review-pr` missed** — `fold_relation` undo issued `RemoveRelation(new_edge.id)` where the folded id is A's *pre-existing* edge, so undoing a merge that folded an edge deleted A's own edge (reachable when two merged entities share a relation to a common neighbour). **Folded** + two sibling undo-correctness fixes surfaced the same pass: a folded `add_relation` undo no longer deletes the pre-existing edge (the add now records `merged_into_existing`), and `remove_relation` undo restores the *full* edge (its before-image is now a full `model_dump`, not subject/predicate/object only — exact confidence/properties; the inverter still tolerates legacy thin rows). **(5) Undo/delete V1 robustness deferred → `docs/BACKLOG.md`** (owner ask, "note what should be done to make it more robust"): undo depth cap; one `created_at` per operation (clock-independent stack head); undo should *report* what open-world churn left unrestored; harden the delete snapshot against a mid-delete crash; collapse `_merge_rows`/`_delete_rows`; O(1) generation lookup. **No spec amendment** — §3.4 (delete) + §10 q2 (undo) were amended in S39; ADR 0007 covers the contract (re-merge resolution recorded into its Consequences). **Checks:** 459 backend pass + ruff/`mypy --strict` clean; frontend build/lint/test green; CI green; both review gates ran; owner gave the per-merge OK.
- **2026-06-20 — Session 41 (governance only — PLAN_SHORT slimming; no feature code).** **(1) `PLAN_SHORT.md` policy tightened to *current-milestone-only*** (owner). The Session-39 rule kept "current + immediately-prior milestone's Done tail", but even one prior milestone left the file at ~365 KB — over the **256 KB single-read limit** (it could no longer be read in one pass). Owner directed: PLAN_SHORT carries the **current milestone only**; all older milestones live in `docs/PLAN_ARCHIVE.md`, archived-and-referenced, **as a standing milestone-roll ritual step** (not a one-off). *Considered & rejected:* keeping M3 as "prior context" (still over the limit); a harder mid-milestone prune of struck cross-cutting/Blocked items (error-prone — deferred to the roll's §3 re-curation, where the whole list is walked anyway). **(2) `docs/AGENTS.md` §7 amended** to match (current-only; archive convention = newest-batch-on-top, verbatim reverse-chron within a batch; what-never-moves clarified). **(3) Ritual wired** (owner, raised S39): `/wrap-session` **step 5c** does/offers the roll-time archive move; `/resume-session` **step 3d** flags bloat (>~200 KB) as a backstop. **(4) First archive batch executed:** M3 + M2 + M1/M0 task sections, Decided, and Done → `docs/PLAN_ARCHIVE.md` (move-not-delete, §4; verified byte-for-byte — dated-bullet count 116 = 18 kept + 98 archived, no duplicates). `PLAN_SHORT.md` **368 KB → ~134 KB**. **Checks:** docs/governance only — no code, no deps; code gates n/a.
- **2026-06-20 — Session 40 (M4.S3b-be1 built + merged, PR #102).** The first M4.S3b backend slice — entity↔entity **merge** — shipped. **(1) Scope: be1 (merge) only** (owner-chosen — took the pre-authorized be1/be2 cut up front; the by-hand property-conflict resolution DM-S3b-2 enlarged merge, and undo can't be tested until merge first writes grouped rows). Delete + the undo executor are **be2**. **(2) Two build-time refinements beyond the resolved register, recorded in ADR 0007:** (a) `graph_edits` gained a **`project_id` column** so the undo stack is project-scoped (the resolved register didn't name it); (b) `repoint_entity_mentions` **returns the moved mention ids** (`RETURNING id`) so the before-image re-points *exactly* those rows back on undo (INV-3 completeness). **(3) Write order refined at build (the `/code-review` fold): delete B *last*** — fold A + re-point edges → re-point mentions → delete B → evidence. The resolved DM-S3b-4 said "Neo4j-then-Postgres"; deleting B first opened a window where its mentions were orphaned and the retry hit `EntityNotFound` (unrecoverable), so the build keeps B alive until the final graph write (still serving DM-S3b-4's retryable-not-half-merge intent); evidence rows reordered to match so undo recreates B before re-pointing mentions. **(4) Known be2 design point (ADR 0007):** the deterministic `uuid5(merge:B:A)` operation id collides if the same pair is re-merged after a be2 undo recreates B — undo must delete an undone op's rows (or add a nonce). **(5) `/review-pr` folds:** dedupe incident edges (a self-loop is returned twice by the undirected neighbourhood query); restrict `resolved_properties` to detected conflict keys (no silent property injection). **ADR 0007** landed (owner-confirmed); INV-9 grep guard widened (+`delete_entity`); INV-3 grouped-log note; relation/candidate lifecycle notes extended. *Considered & not done:* generalizing `_merge_rows` for be2 (YAGNI until be2 lands), parallelizing the neighbourhood reads (PoC scale). **Checks:** 427 backend pass + ruff/mypy clean; frontend lint/build/test clean; CI green; both review gates ran.

- **2026-06-19 — Session 37 (M4.S3a-be built + merged, PR #96).** **(1) DM-S3a-3 resolved-at-build to a *direct* edge-writer (option b) — the one decision that changed from the register's recorded lean.** The register's first choice routed a manual relation-add through `RelationReviewService.decide` to keep it the sole edge-writer; at build the `verify-at-build` falsified that — `decide` resolves an edge's endpoints by **surface-name-within-a-paragraph** (`_resolve` keys on `(paragraph_id, normalized_name)`), which a hand-picked edge between two arbitrary accepted entities has neither of, so a synthetic `staged_relations` row would mean fabricating a paragraph + names that round-trip to the chosen ids. Owner approved the register's **pre-authorized fallback (b)**: `EntityEditService` writes edges **directly** (`create_relation` reused for add, a new `delete_relation`). Consequence: **INV-9's edge-writer set grows too**, under the same "only human-reached handlers" rewording (not just nodes). Recorded in **ADR 0006**, the register DM-S3a-3, OQ-23, and `invariants.md`. *Considered & rejected:* forcing the synthetic-staged-row path (fragile, dishonest). **(2) DM-S3a-2 verify-at-build → one `graph_edits` table** for both node-field and edge edits (`target_kind` discriminates), columns `(target_id, target_kind, op, before, after, actor, created_at)`. **(3) Evidence-loss-on-crash window accepted as the disclosed PoC posture (DM-S3a-6 LWW):** graph-write-first/evidence-last means a crash between them leaves the edit applied but unlogged; documented in the `EntityEditService` docstring + ADR 0006 (one local author; undo-execution is a later slice). **(4) Review-gate fixes folded:** `/review-pr` — a blank `predicate` reached `GraphRelation`'s validator as an uncaught `ValidationError` → **500**, fixed to a boundary **422**; `/code-review` — the predicate validator returned the *unstripped* value (`"  LOVES  "` → a forked `uuid5` edge id + padded Neo4j type), now **stripped** to match how `apply_entity_edit` strips entity `type`. *Considered & left as-is:* the 3-copy `_now()` helper + a Postgres-store base class (out-of-scope drive-by refactors); the idempotent duplicate-add no-op and undirected delete-by-unique-id (by-design). **(5) Retro: no skill/`CLAUDE.md` change.** Observed that the vault's *derived* notes (`INDEX.md`/`CHANGELOG.md`/`overview.md`) read stale post-ADR-0006 (they describe the S36 pre-build state) — but they are architect-regenerated (not hand-edited, per `architecture/AGENTS.md`), so the fix is a near-term `meta-architect:review-architecture` re-sync, **not** a new rule (auto-running the architect from a ritual is the wiring ADR 0002 defers). - **2026-06-19 — Session 36 (M4.S3a scope + step-0 decompose + register resolved; backlog additions; vault-only, no production code).** **(1) Backlog additions (owner).** Recorded two forward-looking post-PoC directions in `docs/BACKLOG.md`: **world graph from multiple sources / attributable knowledge** (the non-fiction/research use case — multiple sources that corroborate/disagree, no single ground truth → every claim attributed to its source; grounded in the existing per-mention provenance ADR 0005, the context-dependent cross-source-identity hazard, and spec §10 q3) and **timeline / temporal qualification of relations & properties** (the "when does Garret wear the cloak" need; anchored to the spec's latent `Event` node type + the M4.S2b occurrence-order list, with a *forward-compatibility* note tying it to "get the baseline graph right" — model relations now so a validity interval / event anchor / source attribution can be hung on them later). *Note:* basic world-graph/multi-story is already in the M4 plan; whether *multi-source attribution* is pulled into PoC scope is a future owner scope-call (stop-and-amend flow), recorded as a direction, not scheduled. **(2) "Manual correction in the reader" sliced by write-risk, lowest-first (owner).** **S3a** = *the side panel becomes editable* — edit an accepted entity's `canonical_name`/`aliases`/`type`/`properties` + add/edit/remove relations between accepted entities (no merge, no re-point, no new spans). **S3b** = entity↔entity **merge** (+ the long-flagged DM-Rel-5 written-edge & `entity_mentions.entity_id` re-point + DM-Rel-6 idempotency) + whole-entity **delete** + **undo-merge**. **S3c** = manual **tag** from selection / **un-tag** / **change boundaries** (reopens the DM-IH-1 span-storage decision). - **2026-06-18 — Session 32 (M4.S1 backend + python-multipart waiver drop): inline-highlights span resolution decided by verifying the data first; the read-only backend shipped; a soak-date-floor rule folded.** **(1) DM-IH-1 — span resolution = render-time string search over name + aliases (owner, after a verify-first detour).** The owner chose "decide after I verify" over committing to an option blind; the verification settled it: the accept path (`candidate_review.py`) writes the mention with **null** `span_start/end`, the staged candidate carries no offset, and the spaCy `CandidateSpan` lives on a separate unlinked path — so the proposal's option (b) "persist the span we already have" was **illusory** (there is no span at accept time). And aliases *accumulate* the prose's surface forms (every merge-accept calls `add_alias(target, candidate_name)`), so an inflected form that was itself extracted+merged becomes a searchable alias — render-time search over canonical + aliases is materially stronger than the decompose assumed. *Considered & rejected:* persist-spans-now (no span to persist; a backend+data change in the slice the owner picked *because* it was low-risk UI), and a verify-build-measure hybrid up front (the verify already answered it). **(2) DM-IH-3 = plain `<mark>` renderer** (owner) — Tiptap/ProseMirror arrives with the manual-annotation slice where editing begins; *rejected:* adopt Tiptap now (ceremony ahead of need for a read-only view). **(3) DM-IH-2/4/7/8 built as proposed** — story-scoped `GET /stories/{id}/reader` doing the cross-store join + a tooltip catalog of only the entities that appeared; longest-match overlap; accepted-only (the read-side echo of INV-1, since mentions are written only by the accept path); tooltip = name+type+aliases. **DM-IH-5/6 (colour, perf)** deferred to the frontend slice (confirm-at-build). **No spec amendment** — §3.5 already specifies the reader; the slice is a read-only projection. **(4) `/code-review` caught a real crash `/review-pr` missed (5th consecutive substantive PR — #36/#60/#63/#78/#81):** the resolver matched against a *casefolded copy* of the paragraph, but casefold can change length on an expanding codepoint (ß→ss, İ→i̇), pushing an offset past the original text → `IndexError`/500 on the whole reader endpoint. Fixed by matching against the **original** text via `re.IGNORECASE` (+ `re.escape` so a name's regex metachars stay literal); regression-tested. **(5) python-multipart OSV waiver dropped (PR #82)** — the S31-deferred fix-first drop: 0.0.31 cleared its 14-day soak, bumped via `/add-dependency`, `GHSA-v9pg-7xvm-68hf` removed from `osv-scanner.toml` + `WAIVERS.md`; OSV scan clean, nothing unmasked. **(6) Retro (1 change, owner approved — soak-date floor):** a dated "drop when (soaks)" must be a **floor** = fixed-version publication date **+ (soak_days + 1)** (package + **15**, image + **8**), because the age gate (`check_dependency_age.py`: `NOW − 14d`) is **time-precise to the second** while a bare `+14` date is intra-day optimistic — this session a 0.0.31 published 06-04 08:27 UTC was still ~53 min too young at the recorded 06-18 drop date. Folded into `/triage-advisory` step 3 + the `infra/osv/WAIVERS.md` header. *Considered & rejected:* a "re-check on the drop day" note (weaker — still surprises); retro-editing the existing starlette dates (the drop-revisit re-runs the real age check anyway). The two other lessons **confirmed existing rules** (no change): `/code-review`-for-substantive-code worked (caught the crash), and verify-first (the deterministic-over-LLM instinct) paid off. **Reviews:** `/review-pr` (self) + `/code-review` (high, 7-angle); 347 backend tests green; both PRs CI 4/4 green, squash-merged.

- **2026-06-24 — Session 54: M4 multi-story LIVE SMOKE = PASS → M4 is feature-complete; a silently-truncated sample story repaired without losing confirmed work; 10 graph-quality findings + 1 spec-drift harvested (no production code; docs-only).** The end-to-end browser/API verification of the multi-story feature shipped across S51 (opener) + S52 (backend) + S53 (frontend). **Verified working:** the `/projects` picker; **adding a second story into an existing project** (oakhaven-2 → Oakhaven, `story_count` 1→2); **cross-story deduplication** (the new story's candidates matched against the project's already-accepted graph — 56 merge proposals resolving to 24 existing entities); and the §3.4 **"this story / whole project" graph toggle** filtering both nodes and edges correctly (a story view is a strict subset of the project view, and the project view is identical from either story). The owner confirmed the toggle live in the browser. **A real bug surfaced mid-smoke:** the LLM auto-chunker had **silently dropped Chapter Six's content** from oakhaven-2 (it kept the chapter heading but none of its paragraphs, and reported success), so the story was truncated and those scenes were never extracted. Since the app has no re-structure or delete-story capability yet, and a clean re-do would have discarded all the entity/relation review the owner had just done, we repaired it **incrementally**: a verified, dry-run-checked database insert of exactly the 6 missing paragraphs (their text taken from the story's complete raw source via the real manual parser), then a **resume-extraction that processed only those 6 paragraphs** (the pipeline's per-paragraph checkpoint skipped the 19 already done). The owner reviewed the small new Chapter-Six batch; the story is now complete (25 paragraphs) with every earlier confirmation intact. **The smoke doubled as a graph-quality review** — ten findings went to `docs/BACKLOG.md` (the auto-chunker's silent content loss being the most serious — `manual` is the only trustworthy structuring mode until it's fixed; plus relation-card-shows-no-source-context, merge-target-needs-a-quote, the homonymy "two different crews" false-merge, modality/arity/eventive-vs-stative relation-modelling gaps, predicate-merge, and the graph as a direct editing surface), and one **spec drift** (the spaCy PreNER baseline is documented as an active pipeline step but is dormant — the live extraction is LLM-only) routed to the cross-cutting list as a stop-and-amend. **Process:** the retrospective reflection turned up nothing needing a rule/skill change; the owner concluded the session. **M4 is now feature-complete, which completes all of V1 (the ingest→graph→viewer PoC); the V1→next-phase milestone roll is deferred to its own conversation** (it's a strategic direction call plus the `PLAN_SHORT` archive move, better done fresh). **Checks:** docs-only — no code or dependencies changed, so the code CI gates don't apply; the running application was the verification surface.
- **2026-06-24 — Session 53: M4 multi-story FRONTEND slice shipped (PR #130) + oakhaven-2 sample (PR #131); both merged, `main` green. M4 multi-story is now complete end-to-end (opener S51 · backend S52 · frontend S53).** The slice that makes multi-story *visible* (spec §3.4/§3.6), built **test-first** on the S52 backend with no backend or generated-client change. **What landed:** `useProjects` + `useProjectStories` query hooks (the new `GET /projects` + `/projects/{id}/stories` surface); a `scope` param on `useStoryGraph` (`story` default | `project`); optional `projectId` on `useUploadStory`; a **`ProjectPicker`** at `/projects` (list projects → select → list stories → open graph/reader, or **add a story** into the same project); the §3.4 **this-story/whole-project graph toggle** on `GraphViewer`; and the **add-story-into-project** flow on `UploadScreen`. **Owner scope call at resume:** include add-story (not read-only), so a project can gain a 2nd story through the UI and the toggle is demonstrable. **The dual review gate earned its keep again:** `/review-pr` (self) found nothing blocking; the heavier **`/code-review` (high, 8 finders) caught 3 real bugs the self-review missed** — (1) the add-to-project target lived only in router `location.state` and was lost on reload, silently downgrading to a *new-project* upload (moved to a URL query param); (2) `useUploadStory` invalidated none of the project caches it dirties, so the picker showed stale `story_count`/lists for the 30 s `staleTime` (now invalidates `projects` + `project-stories` off the response `project_id`); (3) the scope toggle didn't reset the selected node, blanking the details panel when narrowing scope (now resets). All folded with tests. **Deferred (owner-approved → `docs/BACKLOG.md`):** cross-story project-scope graph-cache coherence (a graph edit invalidates only the edited story's prefix, leaving a sibling story's project-scoped view stale 30 s; self-healing, the broad fix touches ~11 mutation hooks). **The oakhaven-2 sample** (continuation of Oakhaven, Chapters 4–5, deliberate coreference cases for multi-story testing) shipped as its own docs-only PR (#131), split out per "don't scope-creep". **Retro → 2 frontend lessons encoded (owner-approved):** (a) `frontend/AGENTS.md` — context that must survive a reload/deep-link goes in the **URL, not router `location.state`** (earned by bug #1); (b) `frontend/src/lib/api/AGENTS.md` — a mutation invalidates **every** cache its write dirties, not just the obvious one (earned by bug #2). **Lesson:** the self-review structurally couldn't catch the reload/cache/selection bugs (they're cross-flow state, not local logic) — the multi-agent `/code-review` is exactly the net for that class, and this is fresh evidence toward making it a *required* gate for substantive UI (the open Blocked question). **Next: the live multi-story browser smoke** (upload oakhaven-2 into the Oakhaven project via the picker, flip the scope toggle on a genuinely 2-story project), then — if clean — the M4→next-milestone roll. **Checks:** frontend 306 pass + lint/format/build clean; no deps changed; CI green on all four jobs for both PRs; owner gave the per-merge OK.
- **2026-06-24 — Session 52: M4 multi-story BACKEND slice shipped (PR #128, merged, `main` green).** The narrowed multi-story capability's backend, built **test-first** straight from the resolved register (DM-MS-1..4 — no new decompose; the proposal *was* the build spec).
