- **2026-06-22 — Session 45: M4.S3c-be shipped — manual tag / un-tag / change-boundaries backend (PR #111, merged).** The backend for "manual correction in the reader" (spec §3.5) — the last of the three write-risk-sliced families (S3a edit · S3b merge/delete/undo · **S3c**). The dominating problem the M4.S1 design left: a rendered highlight is a *live search hit with no saved identity*, so a hand-tagged span (an inflected form, a pronoun, a brand-new entity) can't be re-found by search and "this highlight is wrong" has no row to delete. The resolved model — **"save only what you touch"** — keeps the live search for auto highlights and adds, incrementally, only what the author actually touches: a manual tag persists a **stored span** (real char offsets, marked `source='manual'`) that overlays and wins over search; a rejected highlight writes a **suppression** record the resolver subtracts; changing a boundary on a search hit *materializes* just that occurrence. No data migration, and the M4.S1 "rename re-highlights for free" behaviour is preserved. Built test-first: a **pure reconciling resolver** (`reconcile_highlights` = search ∪ manual − suppressions, manual-wins-then-longest-match — the first failing test); a **§6.4 schema amendment** (a `source` column + a `mention_suppressions` table, taken through the stop-and-amend flow first); five write operations on the existing edit service (**tag an existing entity, tag a brand-new entity, "not an entity", "not this entity", change boundaries**); and full **undo** integration — every correction is reversible through the existing story-scoped Undo, with the inverters **tested against the writer's real recorded output** (not a hand-built fixture) so a producer/consumer drift can't hide. Tagging can **create a new accepted entity** directly (a new human-reached graph writer — INV-9's enumeration grows, its sixth witnessed instance). `ADR 0008` records the storage model + the reconciliation contract; INV-9 reconciled across the vault. **Both review gates ran:** the self-review found nothing blocking; the heavier multi-agent `/code-review` found **zero correctness bugs** and surfaced one cleanup (a deterministic-id formula repeated four times — folded into a shared helper so undo-by-id can't drift). One build-time refinement, recorded in the ADR: rejection is handled **uniformly as a suppression** (even over a manual tag) rather than deleting rows — one mechanism, one inverse. **Surfaced a follow-up** (owner ask): the §6.4 schema sketch omits the `entity_mentions.embedding` column M3 already added — to be reconciled, and its PoC scope decided, in its own near-term session (Blocked/questions). **Next: M4.S3c-fe** — the Tiptap read-only reader + selection + right-click menu + tag picker (DM-S3c-7), the slice that makes all of this usable in the browser. **Checks:** backend 523 pass + ruff/`mypy --strict` clean; frontend 247 pass + lint/format/build clean; CI green on all four jobs; owner gave the per-merge OK.
- **2026-06-22 — Session 44: M4.S3c scoped + decomposed + register RESOLVED; M4 multi-story scope re-cut (design/planning only — no production code).** The next slice's full design pass, plus owner scope decisions that reshaped the rest of M4. **(1) M4.S3c — manual tag / un-tag / change-boundaries decomposed** (`meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0 → `architecture/proposals/m4-s3c-manual-tagging.md`, `accepted`, register **DM-S3c-1..9 / OQ-26 RESOLVED**). It's the final "manual correction in the reader" slice (after S3a edit + S3b merge/delete/undo). The dominating finding: a rendered highlight today is a render-time **search hit with no saved identity** (the M4.S1 design left `entity_mentions` offsets NULL and searches the prose live), so a manually-tagged span (an inflected form, a pronoun, a brand-new entity) can't be re-found by search, and "this highlight is wrong" has no stored row to delete. **Owner resolved the storage model = "save only what you touch"** (keep the live search for auto highlights; persist real offsets only for spots tagged/corrected by hand; record a small suppression note for a rejected highlight — incremental, no data migration, the M4.S1 "rename re-highlights for free" behaviour preserved), plus: tagging can **create new entities** (not just attach to existing), corrections are **undoable** via the existing story-scoped Undo, and — overriding the architect's lean — **adopt the Tiptap editor now** so the V2 text-editing features inherit a robust selection engine. - **2026-06-22 — Session 43: M4.S3b-fe shipped — merge/delete/undo reader UI (PR #107, merged) — and a backend merge-undo bug it surfaced, fixed (PR #108, merged). M4.S3b is COMPLETE end-to-end.** The frontend for the graph-mutation routes, test-first in the S3a-fe rhythm (pure mapper → hook → component): `mergeConflicts.ts` (by-hand property-conflict resolver computed *client-side* from both entities' properties, because the merge 400 carries only conflicting key names, not values — mirrors the backend's `detect_property_conflicts`); `useMergeEntities`/`useDeleteEntity`/`useUndo` (undo invalidates the reader/graph/detail caches only on a *real* apply, never on a preview); `MergeControls` (reuse `EntityPicker` → conflict resolver → confirm → `MergeSummaryResponse` counts; self-merge blocked client-side); delete-with-confirm in `ReaderEntityPanel` (closes the panel on success); `UndoButton` in the reader *header* (undo is **story-scoped** — owner call) with preview→confirm→apply and 404 (nothing to undo) / 409 (drift) handling. CI had stayed green because the inverter's unit test hand-built a fixture with the op name the writer never emits. - **2026-06-20 — Session 42: M4.S3b-be2 shipped — whole-entity delete + the general undo executor (PR #105, merged). INV-3 moves from *recorded* to *executed*.** be1 wrote the grouped, append-only `graph_edits` log; be2 consumes it. **Delete:** `EntityEditService.delete_entity` removes an accepted entity, its relations, and its text occurrences (real `DETACH DELETE` + a full before-image snapshot — node + incident edges + mentions), recorded as one grouped reversible operation; `DELETE /stories/{id}/entities/{eid}` (204/404/503). **Undo:** `undo_last` → `POST …/graph-edits/undo` (undo-last) reverses the newest live operation — reads it, inverts it in reverse `seq` via the pure `domain/graph_undo.invert_operation`, runs a drift check (refuse → 409 if the target was edited/re-created since), applies each inverse through the same human-reached writers, then stamps it `undone`; `?preview=true` reports *what would be reversed* without acting (DM-S3b-1 see-what-I-undo). Read path: `PostgresEditStore.latest_live_operation` (project-scoped; `COALESCE(operation_id, id)` so S3a singleton edits are undoable too) + `mark_operation_undone`. **Two design points from ADR 0007 settled:** DM-S3b-5 survivor-delete = allow + drift-refuse (owner-confirmed); the re-do-after-undo `uuid5` id collision = a generation discriminator that keeps the `undone_at` stamp model (recorded back into ADR 0007's Consequences). **Architecture:** INV-3 *executed* + INV-9 fifth witnessed instance in `invariants.md`; new `state-machines/graph-operation.md` (`applied → undone`); INDEX updated. **Reviews — the two-gate rule paid off again (6th+ substantive PR):** `/review-pr` (self) flagged the doc reconciliation + crash-window notes; **`/code-review` (multi-agent, high) caught a real data-loss bug** — `fold_relation` undo deleted the survivor's pre-existing edge — plus two sibling undo-fidelity issues, all folded with regression tests (incl. a fold-undo integration test). Undo/delete V1 robustness items (depth cap, clock-independent stack head, unrestored-churn signal, mid-delete-crash hardening, row-factory dedup) recorded in `docs/BACKLOG.md` at the owner's request. **Checks:** 459 backend pass + ruff/`mypy --strict` clean; frontend build/lint/test green; CI green. **Lesson:** the documented "run `/code-review` in addition to `/review-pr` on substantive destructive write-paths because a missed bug is costly and the Codex net is thin" rule earned its keep yet again — the fold data-loss bug was exactly the cross-file/edge-case class a single self-review structurally can't catch. **Next: M4.S3b-fe** (merge flow UI + delete-with-confirm + an undo affordance that previews what it reverses). **Retro → one ritual tightening (owner-approved): neutral waiver-soak framing in the handoff.** The resume brief misread the starlette waivers as "soaked / actionable" when their drop-floor dates were days in the *future* — caused by the prior handoff's pre-judged "DUE THIS WEEK / should have soaked by now" wording (the soak-equivalent of a false infra anchor — it goes stale, and acting on it bumps a dep still inside its 14-day soak, a §6.7 misstep). Fixed both halves: **`/wrap-session` step 7** now requires waiver lines to state a *neutral floor date to compute against* ("droppable on YYYY-MM-DD"), never a verdict; **`/resume-session` step 3b** now says compute drop-readiness from the floor date vs today, don't inherit the handoff's framing. *Considered & rejected:* a rule for the pre-commit `ruff-format`-aborts-a-commit micro-friction (self-correcting — the hook is its own safety net). The two-gate review catching the fold data-loss bug *confirmed* the existing rule (no change).

- **2026-06-18 — Session 34: M4.S2 slice chosen + decomposed, and M4.S2a backend shipped (PR #89).** The owner-chosen second M4 slice (the **entity side panel**, spec §3.4/§3.5), all in one session: choice → step-0 decompose → backend build → review → merge. **(1) Slice choice (owner):** side panel over manual-correction-in-reader — the read-only inspection surface (an entity's neighbourhood + occurrences + properties) is what you need to *judge* a correction, so it lands before the edit tools; manual correction is the next slice. **(2) `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0** → `architecture/proposals/m4-side-panel.md` (`accepted`, register **DM-SP-1..8 / OQ-22** resolved with the owner same session), + glossary `ego-graph`, learning-log ×2. Build-time refinement: occurrences left to the frontend (DM-SP-3), so the endpoint is exactly `properties` + ego-graph (the M4.S1 one-pure-fn-+-one-endpoint shape). Read-only — INV-1/INV-9 untouched, no LLM. **(4) Reviews:** `/review-pr` (×2, self — clean) + `/code-review` (high, 7 finder angles) **folded one should-fix** — two finders independently flagged the neighbourhood query not project-scoping the *neighbour* (unlike `get_relations`); now `WHERE n.project_id = e.project_id` (§6.4 defense-in-depth) + a cross-project-exclusion test, and the defensive guard made load-bearing with a test. Nits (domain models as DTOs, single-404 description) left as deliberate pattern-consistent choices. **(5) Backlog note (owner idea):** `docs/BACKLOG.md` — the reader as the paragraph-by-paragraph working surface (extract/merge/add/remove in-prose), with the open local-vs-cross-text relationship question to think through post-PoC. **Checks:** 361 backend + 164 frontend tests green; ruff/format/mypy/eslint/build clean; CI 4/4 green; squash-merged on the owner's per-merge OK. **Lessons:** (a) decompose + build in one session worked cleanly when context stayed healthy — the step-0 decompose still earned its place (it surfaced the assembly-vs-new-data framing that shaped the slice); (b) `/code-review` again added a real should-fix the single `/review-pr` missed (the project-scoping gap) — the multi-agent pass keeps paying for substantive code; (c) a build-time *refinement* of an approved decision (occurrences → frontend) is legitimate and expected — the decompose's `verify-at-build` markers anticipated it; record it where the decision lives.

- **2026-06-18 — Session 33: M3→M4 vault sync (PR #85) + M4.S1 inline-highlights **frontend** (PR #86), live-verified end-to-end; a post-PoC backlog file split out.** **(1) Vault-first (PR #85, `2f361ff`).** Cleared the carried open-block B with a `meta-architect:*` pass: drew `architecture/state-machines/relation-lifecycle.md` (the edge-gate twin; closes OQ-20), flipped `proposals/m4-inline-highlights.md` → `accepted` with the whole DM-IH register annotated resolved-as-built (OQ-21), fixed the `glossary/model-tier-routing.md` "not yet built" drift; `/review-pr` (incl. an explicit §2 decision-state sweep) clean; faithful surprise recorded (`held`/`committable` are derived, not persisted). **(2) M4.S1 frontend (PR #86, `2795ae1`), test-first.** `frontend/src/features/text-reader/`: a pure paragraph-splitter (`segments.ts`) + colour-by-type (`palette.ts`: fixed common-type palette + deterministic hash fallback honouring open-world INV-4 + a legend) + `useReader` query hook + `ParagraphText` `<mark>` renderer with a name+type+aliases tooltip (React-escaped) + `Legend` + the `/stories/:storyId/reader` route + a graph-viewer link. Strict TDD for the pure logic (splitter/palette red→green); components shaped-then-tested (disclosed). 164 frontend tests; tsc/eslint/prettier clean. `/review-pr` folded 2 coverage gaps; `/code-review` (high, 7-angle) found **no confirmed bug** (overlap/zero-length highlights impossible per the backend resolver's guards; `Math.abs(INT_MIN)` is a positive double in JS). **(3) Live smoke test — the whole pipeline, end to end.** Wrote the Oakhaven story from scratch (`docs/samples/oakhaven.md`) and ran upload → manual chunk (3 ch/6 sc) → extract (free Ollama cloud, ~9% session quota) → review/dedup (incl. correctly **rejecting** the Elira↔Elara false-positive merge) → relations → reader. The reader rendered highlights, colour-by-type+legend, tooltips, multi-surface-form entities via aliases, longest-match — *and* the honest failure modes (missed-coref "the magistrate" as its own node; un-highlightable hallucinated "broken table"). **(4) Backlog file (retro change).** Created **`docs/BACKLOG.md`** for concrete post-PoC items, migrated ~12 out of `PLAN_LONG.md` (kept strategic), and wired its routing rule into root `AGENTS.md`, `docs/AGENTS.md`, `/wrap-session`, `/review-pr`. **Checks:** 164 frontend tests green; lint/format/build clean; both feature PRs CI green, two review passes each, squash-merged on per-merge owner OK. **Lessons:** (a) **a live end-to-end test is irreplaceable** — it surfaced ~12 real product gaps (coreference, extraction hallucination, monotone re-match ordering, near-name discrimination, the reader-as-correction-surface) that a green suite never would, and concretely killed the auto-commit idea (two different sisters scored 0.91 > the 0.85 flip line — auto-commit would have silently fused them; the human gate caught what similarity can't); (b) the post-PoC backlog outgrew `PLAN_LONG`'s "strategic, stable" remit, so it earned a dedicated, wired-in home; (c) `/resume-session` again caught a real drift (a stale `features/reader/` path in the handoff vs the `features/text-reader/` convention) before any code. **(5) Mid-wrap, the frontend `npm audit` gate red on a newly-surfaced HIGH undici advisory** (dev-only via jsdom, unreachable, no soaked fix). Triaged via `/triage-advisory`; owner's §6.7 call = scope the gate to shipped deps (`npm audit --omit=dev`) — spec §6.7 amended, reconciled across `ci.yml` + the skills + an orienting vault note; also bumped `react-router-dom` 7.15→7.16 to clear a LOW CSRF (PR #88, `c335801`). Lesson: a security gate should reflect *shipped* risk — narrowing scope is the principled escape hatch for an unreachable dev-dep advisory with no soaked fix.

- **2026-06-18 — Session 32: M4.S1 inline-highlights **backend** shipped (PR #81) + the python-multipart OSV waiver dropped (PR #82).** The first M4 ("V1 polish") feature code, the read-only side of inline highlights (spec §3.5). **(1) Resolved the DM-IH register with the owner by verifying the data first.** The owner chose "decide after I verify" on the gating call (DM-IH-1 span resolution); the verification found the accept path writes the mention with **null** char offsets and the spaCy span is gone by accept time — so the decompose's "persist the existing span" option was *illusory* — while aliases accumulate the prose's actual surface forms (each merge-accept adds one), making **render-time string search over canonical_name + aliases** both the only zero-data-change option *and* stronger on inflection than assumed. DM-IH-3 = a plain `<mark>` renderer (Tiptap deferred to manual annotation). **(2) Built the backend test-first:** a pure `domain/highlights.py` span resolver (word-boundary, case-insensitive, longest-match-wins overlap, omit-on-miss fail-closed) + a story-scoped `GET /stories/{id}/reader` that cross-joins Postgres paragraphs+mentions × Neo4j entities in app code and returns per-paragraph highlight ranges + a tooltip catalog of only the entities that appeared + a bulk `list_entity_mentions_for_story` loader. 12 unit + 4 integration tests; mypy `--strict` clean; OpenAPI + typed TS client regenerated. **(3) The layered review gate paid off a 5th consecutive substantive PR (#36/#60/#63/#78/#81):** `/review-pr` (self) read clean, but the 7-angle `/code-review` caught a real crash it missed — the resolver matched against a *casefolded copy*, which can change length on an expanding codepoint (ß→ss, İ→i̇) and push an offset past the original text → `IndexError`/500 on the whole reader endpoint; fixed by matching the original text via `re.IGNORECASE` (+ `re.escape` for literal name metachars), regression-tested. **(4) Dropped the python-multipart waiver (PR #82):** the S31-deferred fix-first drop once 0.0.31 cleared its 14-day soak — bumped via `/add-dependency`, removed `GHSA-v9pg-7xvm-68hf` from `osv-scanner.toml` + `WAIVERS.md`; OSV scan clean, nothing unmasked. **(5) Retro — a soak-date-floor rule:** record a dated "drop when (soaks)" as publication-date **+ (soak_days + 1)** (package +15, image +8), since the age gate is time-precise to the second while a bare +14 date is intra-day optimistic — this session a fix published 06-04 08:27 UTC was still ~53 min too young at the recorded 06-18 drop date, forcing a ~50-min wait. Folded into `/triage-advisory` step 3 + `infra/osv/WAIVERS.md`. **Checks:** 347 backend tests green; ruff/format/mypy/frontend-lint/tsc clean; both PRs CI 4/4 green, squash-merged (#81 `01b2173`, #82 `3f16d5e`). **Not done (carried to next session):** acting on the 2026-06-17 architecture report + OQ-20 (the relation-lifecycle state-machine drawing) + the `glossary/model-tier-routing.md` "not yet built" drift — a `meta-architect:*` vault pass. **Lessons:** (a) *verify before you commit to a design option* — the owner's "decide after I verify" turned a plausible-but-wrong choice (persist spans) into the right one (search) by reading the actual write path; the deterministic-over-LLM instinct, applied to a design decision; (b) `/code-review` caught a self-review miss for the **fifth** consecutive substantive PR — the casefold-length assumption was load-bearing and invisible to a happy-path read; the multi-agent finder's edge-case angle is the safety net the single self-review structurally lacks; (c) a recorded soak *date* is a floor, not the gate — the gate is time-precise, so date arithmetic that ignores the publication time-of-day surprises you by hours on the drop day.

- ~~**LLM router doesn't record/fail-over on a malformed-but-`200` provider envelope.**~~ ✅ **Resolved 2026-06-08 (M2.S3, PR #42):** typed `ProviderResponseError` added in `adapters/llm/base.py`, raised by the Ollama + OpenRouter adapters on a malformed-`200` envelope (missing fields, unparseable body, **and null `content`** — the null case caught by `/code-review`), and `router.py` records a failure row + fails over like a 5xx; the "envelope-malformed vs schema-invalid" split is proven by router tests. Closes the §6.6 "one row per call" gap (INV-5). (M2.S2 own-review should-fix → built M2.S3.)
- ~~**ChunkingAgent doesn't map `ProviderResponseError` (malformed-`200`) to its route's 502.**~~ ✅ **Resolved 2026-06-10 (M2.S4, PR #48):** `ChunkingAgent` now catches `ProviderResponseError` around the provider call → `ChunkingError` (the structure route already maps that to 502), so a malformed-200 during chunking is a 502, not an unhandled 500. + test. Original below. M2.S3 added a typed `ProviderResponseError` (adapters raise it on a malformed-`200` envelope). `ExtractionAgent` is behind the router, which records + fails over; but `ChunkingAgent` holds a *raw* `OllamaProvider` and its retry loop catches only `ValidationError`, so a malformed-`200` during chunking propagates as `ProviderResponseError` past the route's `except ChunkingError` → an unhandled **500**, though `POST /stories/{id}/structure` advertises **502** for LLM failure. **Not a regression** (pre-M2.S3 the same body raised a raw `KeyError` → also 500). Cheap fix: catch `ProviderResponseError` in `ChunkingAgent` → `ChunkingError` (the route already maps that to 502). The deeper fix is to move chunking behind the router like extraction (gets failover + the `llm_calls` row too) — lands naturally with **M2.S4**. (M2.S3 `/code-review` finding, deferred 2026-06-08.)
- ~~**`RelationCandidate` accepts blank `subject`/`predicate`/`object` as success.**~~ ✅ **Resolved 2026-06-10 (M2.S4, PR #48):** added the same non-empty `field_validator` (covering all three fields) used for `candidate_name`, so blank relation output is retried not accepted; + an agent-retry test and a direct-validation test. Original below. `agents/extraction_agent.py:92-94` types the three relation fields as plain `str` with **no non-empty validator** (only `candidate_name` has one). A model returning `{"subject":"","predicate":"","object":"",…}` validates as a successful `ExtractionProposal`, so the agent's retry loop **stops** and the future M2.S4 graph writer gets a relation with no usable endpoint or type. **Distinct from the intentionally-accepted dangling relation** — a dangling endpoint still needs a *non-empty* surface form or id; only its *resolution* (match/create) is deferred to M3. Fix: add the same non-empty `field_validator` used for `candidate_name` to `subject`/`predicate`/`object`, so blank output is retried not accepted; + a test. A real gap **both** M2.S3 review passes missed (tests cover blank `candidate_name` + empty-lists, never blank relation fields). Small — fold into **M2.S4** (where it bites) or a quick standalone PR. (External review remark on merged PR #42, 2026-06-08.)

**Completed-milestone task sections (M3, M2).**

## Completed milestone: Milestone 3 — Cascade matching (dedupe) — feature-complete 2026-06-17

_Retained as history — all sessions done (S1–S4f). M3's outcome: the §3.3 four-stage cascade
**dedupes under full human control** — extraction stages candidates, the human-accept paths are the
only graph writers (nodes **and** relation edges), on-accept re-match + manual handpick keep a single
ingest's graph clean. Retired INV-8; landed INV-1's enforcers (nodes + edges) + INV-9. §9 M3's "dedupe
works, I control every decision, the graph is clean" is met for entities and relations._

**Goal:** the §3.3 four-stage cascade so duplicate candidates become **one** entity
under the author's control — *"dedupe works, I control every decision, the graph is
clean"* (§9 M3). Stage 1 RapidFuzz → Stage 2 embedding cosine → Stage 3 LLM
`JudgeAgent` → Stage 4 human review queue. M3 **retires the temporary INV-8** (no
dedupe) and lands **INV-1's** first enforcer (the human gate).

**Design:** framed in the step-0 decompose — `architecture/proposals/m3-cascade-matching.md`
(milestone register **DM1–DM6 + DM7 + DM-rej all resolved** — DM1–DM4 S20, DM6 S19, DM5 S22,
DM7/DM-rej S23) + the S4a backend decompose `architecture/proposals/m3s4a-intercept-write-path.md`
(build register **DM-S4a-1..5 resolved**, S23) + the candidate-lifecycle state machine
(`architecture/state-machines/candidate-lifecycle.md`, finalises to `living` at S4a).
**DM6 decided (2026-06-11): (A) intercept-before-write** — extraction *stages* candidates,
Neo4j is written only on human accept (so M2.S4's CREATE-on-extract path is refactored).
**The DM6 write-path refactor + INV-8 retirement land with M3.S4a** —
when the human-accept path actually exists; INV-8 stays the live contract until then, and
the cascade is built proposal-only/unwired through M3.S2–S3 (no empty-graph window).

**Feature order** (re-sliced 2026-06-11 / S20 — Stage 1 and Stage 2 split into their own
sessions once the embedding stack's cost surfaced; see Decided):

1. **M3.S1 — `MatchingAgent` Stage 1 (RapidFuzz).** ✅ **DONE (PR #56, 2026-06-11).**
   Deterministic token-set ratio vs `canonical_name` + aliases; routes auto-merge /
   ambiguous / new by the §3.3 bands. Carried **DM1** (threshold home → `config.py`) +
   the **§6.7 HF-model channel** amendment. Proposes only; unwired (INV-1 honoured by
   construction, INV-8 untouched). _Was "Stage 1 + Stage 2"; re-sliced._
2. **M3.S2 — `MatchingAgent` Stage 2 (embeddings) + the `pgvector` read-path switch.**
   ✅ **DONE (PR #58, 2026-06-12).** `postgres_repo.py` `NULL AS embedding` → real
   `vector(768)` + `register_vector_async` (centralised in `db.connect`); per-mention
   vectors on `entity_mentions` (migration); Stage 2 = **max** cosine of candidate-context
   vs the entity's mention vectors (strict `>0.85`). Carried **DM2** (model
   `paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2`, 768-dim, pinned by commit SHA via the §6.7
   HF-channel — `scripts/pin_hf_model.py`) + **DM3/DM4** (storage). Added the embedding
   library stack + the **torch OSV waiver**. **Foundation-only** (see Decided): EmbeddingAgent
   built but *not* wired into the live coordinator (mentions written `embedding=None`) — the
   embed-on-extract wiring lands M3.S4 with the cascade. Verify-at-build passed: model loads
   on the CPU host, emits 768 dims.
3. **M3.S3 — `JudgeAgent` Stage 3.** ✅ **DONE (PR #60, 2026-06-15).** LLM-as-judge
   (cloud_free via the router — `weight="medium"`/`task_type="judge"`; DM5 resolved),
   strict-JSON `{match, confidence, reasoning}` (degenerate body fails + retries),
   prompt-injection-safe, full Appendix C.3 field set. `classify_verdict` merges iff
   `match AND confidence > 0.8` (§3.3 amended with the clarifying merge rule). Carried
   the **rule-of-three fold** (`validate_with_retry` + `TaskWeight`/`Router` → `base.py`).
   Proposal-only/unwired; INV-8 untouched.
**M3.S4 was re-sliced 2026-06-15 (S23) into S4a + S4b** — the decompose
(`architecture/proposals/m3s4a-intercept-write-path.md`) showed the backend write-path refactor +
the React review-queue UI are too big for one conversation. The invariant flip is witnessed at the
**backend/API boundary**, so S4a is a coherent green slice (no empty-graph window) and S4b is purely
additive UI. See Decided 2026-06-15.

4. **M3.S4a — intercept-before-write (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #63, 2026-06-15).** New Postgres
   **`candidates`** staging table + the cascade **wired synchronously into the `ExtractionCoordinator`**
   (embed-on-extract → Matching Stage 1/2 → Judge Stage 3, fail-closed) + the human-accept write-path
   as API endpoints (`GET …/candidates` / accept→MERGE-or-CREATE to Neo4j + `entity_mention`(+vector) +
   a `candidate_decisions` evidence row / reject→remembered). **Retired INV-8 → landed INV-1's first
   enforcer + new INV-9** ("no automated stage writes the graph") + **ADR 0004** + finalised the
   candidate-lifecycle note to `living`, test-first — the flip test ("extraction stages, writes **zero**
   Neo4j nodes; the accept endpoint is the only writer") replaced M2.S4's "two identical → two nodes".
   `create_entity` → idempotent MERGE-on-id; accept path status-flip-last + deterministic ids (idempotent
   retries); store-down→503 + Neo4j-lifespan-close cross-cutting folded in. **Relations are staged
   (JSONB) but the edge write + re-point-on-merge is deferred to S4b.** Register DM-S4a-1..5 resolved
   (Decided 2026-06-15).
5. **M3.S4b — review-queue UI Stage 4 (frontend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #65, 2026-06-15).**
   `features/extraction-review/` with keyboard nav (§3.3 *entity* elements: quote ±200 chars,
   NEW-vs-MERGE, reasoning, top-3 alternatives, accept/change-target/create/reject), consuming S4a's
   endpoints. Keyboard scheme = §8.3 J/K/A/N/M/R (the §10 q9 pick). Hooks (`useCandidates`/
   `useReviewCandidate`, generated-client-typed), a pure keyboard reducer, `CandidateCard` +
   `ReviewQueue`, route + graph-viewer link. Browser-verified end-to-end (22 staged → accept/reject →
   21 nodes, queue drained). **Deferred out of S4b (tracked in cross-cutting):** the **decide-relations
   action + relation-write backend**, and the **§3.4 graph story-vs-project scoping**. **INV-2 consent
   gate deferred past M3** — *not* landed here.
6. **M3.S4c — intra-batch dedup: on-accept live re-match (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #67, 2026-06-15).**
   Decompose: `architecture/proposals/m3s4c-intra-batch-rematch.md` (register DM-S4c-1..6 resolved). Each
   human **accept** now re-runs the **deterministic** matcher (Stage 1 RapidFuzz + Stage 2 cosine, reusing
   the candidate's stored `context_embedding` + the mention vector just written; **no LLM**) over still-pending
   candidates against the just-accepted entity; a strong match (Stage 1 `>85%` **or** Stage 2 `cosine >0.85`)
   flips the staged `proposal` `new → merge` (+ target + provenance/alternatives). **Monotone** (only
   `new → merge`) → idempotent; writes **only the `candidates` table** — **INV-1/INV-9 hold** (re-match is the
   first automated *staging-proposal* writer, never the graph). New `agents/candidate_rematch.py`
   (`ReMatchService` reusing the matcher; match signal built from the accept's own data → **zero extra reads**;
   Stage-1-only when a vector is absent) + `postgres_candidate_store.update_proposal` (`status='review-queued'`
   guard) + an optional `rematch` collaborator on `CandidateReviewService.accept`, **fail-closed**
   (`contextlib.suppress` — a re-match failure never rolls back the accept; reject/replay don't fire it).
   Vault folds: `candidate-lifecycle` self-loop + INV-9 graph-vs-staging clarification; **ADR 0005 declined**
   (see Decided). Backend-only (S4b card already renders merges; queue refetches on accept). Spec §3.3 (amended
   S25). `/review-pr` + `/code-review` clean. Full suite 301 green.
7. **M3.S4d — manual handpick (backend entity-search + picker UI).** ✅ **DONE (PR #70, 2026-06-16).**
   `GET /stories/{id}/entities?q=` (**project-scoped** — DM-S4c-5) over Neo4j accepted entities via
   `Neo4jRepo.list_entities`, ranked with the **same RapidFuzz signal the matcher uses** (a shared
   `_rank` core that `top_alternatives` now delegates to) — **no score floor** (the diminutives
   handpick exists to catch score *below* cross-category noise, so reachability wins; the human picks);
   `q` never reaches Cypher (injection-safe). `EntityPicker` + `useEntitySearch` in the review card feed
   the existing `M`/merge-accept path; **last-pick-wins** (picking an alternative clears a handpick).
   **Supersedes** the deferred "arbitrary-entity search merge target" cross-cutting item. §3.4 scoping
   reconciled (both routes project-scoped). `/code-review` caught a handpick-precedence bug (fixed).
8. **M3.S4e — relation-write (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #76, 2026-06-16).** Resolves each staged relation's
   surface-form endpoints → committed entity ids and writes graph edges under an **explicit human gate**
   (the §3.3 5th action "decide on relations" — DM-Rel-1, owner S28). Built test-first: new `staged_relations`
   table (status lifecycle + evidence — DM-Rel-4), normalised-exact same-paragraph resolution reading the
   committed id from `candidates` (DM-Rel-2; the create-id derivation promoted to the shared
   `domain.candidates.committed_entity_id` helper), `create_relation` `CREATE` → idempotent **MERGE on
   `uuid5(subject_id, predicate, object_id)`** (DM-Rel-6 — one edge per fact across paragraphs, retry-safe),
   `RelationReviewService` (the only edge writer — **INV-1 broadened to edges**, INV-9 second instance) with
   TOCTOU re-resolve + held/self-loop/ambiguous guards (DM-Rel-7), two `decide-relations` endpoints. **ADR
   0005**; DM-Rel-2/4/5/6/7 confirmed at build as proposed. `/code-review` caught + fixed a real bug: a
   *changed* merge target wasn't persisted on the candidate row, so a relation endpoint resolved to the stale
   target — `set_status` now persists the committed target on merge-accept. Re-point of *written* edges stays
   **M4** (DM-Rel-5); per-mention provenance for triple-deduped edges is a post-PoC follow-up (ADR 0005).
9. **M3.S4f — relation-review UI (frontend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #78, 2026-06-17).** The React "decide on
   relations" surface consuming S4e's endpoints — `useRelations` (`GET …/relations`) + `useDecideRelation`
   (`POST …/relations/{id}/decide`, invalidating the graph only on commit), a pure keyboard reducer (J/K
   nav, **A=commit / R=reject** — a §8.3 subset, owner-confirmed S30), `RelationCard` (surface triple +
   confidence, **surface-strings-v1**, owner-confirmed) + `RelationQueue` (window keyboard, per-card
   in-flight disabling, 409 stale-endpoint surface, graph link), route + graph-viewer "Relations" link.
   Mirrors `features/extraction-review/`. Test-first (reducer strict-TDD + card + container + hook).
   Browser-verified end-to-end (commit wrote a Neo4j edge visible in the graph, reject wrote nothing).
   **`/code-review` (6-finder) caught a real bug `/review-pr` missed:** `decideMessage` mapped 409 →
   "already decided", but the backend's 409 is a *stale/held endpoint* (already-decided is a 200) — and the
   test had *masked* it with a fabricated 409 body; fixed + retested, plus two folded test gaps
   (`useDecideRelation` hook test, graph-viewer relations-link assertion). **This closes M3's feature work
   — the §3.3 cascade + both human gates (entities S4a–S4d, edges S4e–S4f) are complete.**

Each ends green + committed; `/review-pr` (+ `/code-review` for substantive code) → PR
→ squash-merge, per feature.

---

## Completed milestone: Milestone 2 — Basic extraction (closed 2026-06-11, M2.S6 / PR #53)

_Retained as history — all six sessions done. M2's outcome: the extraction pipeline is
visible end-to-end in a browser, **with duplicates** (the no-dedupe INV-8 that M3
lifts)._

**Goal:** turn persisted paragraphs into an entity graph in Neo4j — **without any
dedupe** (every candidate = new entity, per spec §9). End-to-end demonstration of
the agent architecture (PreNER → Extraction → Neo4j write; no Matching/Judge yet —
those are M3), the multi-tier router (cloud_free default, paid cloud configurable,
OpenRouter as meta), and the spec §8.5 agent activity panel + spec §6.6 token /
GPU-time budget visible in the UI.

M2 is split into **6 sessions**, each sized for one Claude Code conversation. Each
ends green (lint/type/tests reported clean) and committed, and leaves a resume
anchor so the next session can pick up by reading this file. Order is by dependency
— do not reorder without updating the handoff block.

---

### Session 1 — PreNERAgent (spaCy, deterministic) `[x]`

_No LLM, no router. Per-paragraph spaCy baseline — spec §7 step 3. The
deterministic-first opener: smallest blast radius, gives M2.S3 a real candidate
set before ExtractionAgent is designed._

- [x] **Deps:** spaCy + `pl_core_news_lg` + `en_core_web_lg` pinned. The model wheels aren't on PyPI, so they became a new §6.7 **direct-URL wheel channel** (GitHub-release wheels, hash-locked in `uv.lock`, soak checked against the asset upload date) rather than going through `/add-dependency`'s PyPI path — spec amended, gate extended. See Decided.
- [x] **Failing test first:** `backend/tests/unit/agents/test_prener_agent.py` (path corrected from the handoff's `backend/tests/…` per `backend/CLAUDE.md` — agent tests live in `tests/unit/agents/`) — PL Appendix B.2 fixture + EN mirror; `PreNERAgent.extract` returns `CandidateSpan`s covering the obvious proper nouns, typed via the spaCy → §3.2 mapping.
- [x] `domain/extraction.py` — `CandidateSpan` (minimal: text, char_start, char_end, spacy_label, mapped_type); no §3.2 full-shape fields.
- [x] `agents/prener_agent.py` — `PreNERAgent.extract(paragraph_text, language)`; lazy per-language model load; PL/EN routing by language (no auto-detect); unsupported language → `ValueError`. Pure `map_spacy_label` + `candidates_from_entities` factored out so the mapping/offset logic is CI-tested without the models.
- [x] Per-paragraph dispatch: candidates returned in-process for the test to assert against (the entity store lands in M2.S4, as planned).

**Done when:** ✅ failing test passes; spaCy + 2 models pinned; PL + EN deterministic fixtures.
**Resume anchor:** ✅ `backend/src/story_forge/agents/prener_agent.py`; `backend/tests/unit/agents/test_prener_agent.py`; spaCy + 2 models (the latter in the optional `models` dependency group) in `backend/pyproject.toml`.

### Session 2 — Paid LLM adapter (OpenRouter) + router + budget tracking `[x]`

_Unlocks every downstream LLM agent. **All in-session decisions now made** (2026-06-02, via the
meta-architect dogfood — see Decided + `docs/decisions/0003` + `architecture/proposals/m2s2-llm-router-budget-cap.md`):
hand-rolled `httpx` adapters (not SDKs); provider order Ollama → OpenRouter → Grok → Anthropic →
Google → OpenAI with **OpenRouter the only paid route built now**; per-day USD cap; control-first
**pause-and-ask** on free-quota-exhaustion or cap (never silent paid escalation)._

- [x] **Grow the seam first:** extend `adapters/llm/base.py` — `CompletionResult` + the `LLMProvider` Protocol carry usage (`model`, `input_tokens`, `output_tokens`, nullable `gpu_seconds`, `cost_estimate`) and the §6.5 `cost_per_1k_tokens` / `rate_limit_kind`; **`adapters/llm/ollama.py` stops discarding** Ollama's `prompt_eval_count`/`eval_count` (INV-5 / OQ-7).
- ~~[ ] `adapters/llm/anthropic.py` — `AnthropicProvider` picked first…~~ **struck 2026-06-02:** not Anthropic-first; direct vendor adapters deferred (OpenRouter covers them). See Decided / ADR 0003.
- ~~[ ] `adapters/llm/openai.py` + `adapters/llm/grok.py` — scaffolded…~~ **struck 2026-06-02:** deferred to "as needed" (was M2.S6 for OpenRouter; vendor stubs no longer scaffolded in S2).
- [x] `adapters/llm/openrouter.py` — `OpenRouterProvider`, hand-rolled `httpx` mirroring `OllamaProvider` (OpenAI-compatible `/chat/completions`, bearer auth, model passthrough, injectable transport). The **first failing test** of the session: this adapter against a mocked transport, asserting the **system-derived usage fields** + a **cap-refusal path** from the start. (Cap-refusal landed as HTTP 402 → `BudgetExceededError`.)
- [x] `adapters/llm/router.py` — `LLMRouter.complete(weight, task_type)` per **amended** §6.5 (orchestrates the call, not `route()→provider` — see Decided): light → cloud_free on a GPU-less host; medium → cloud_free; heavy → cloud_strong preferring OpenRouter. **Error-discriminated** within-tier failover (429/5xx/**transport errors** → fail over; 401 → fail over but not quota; other 4xx → re-raise). Only **pure-429** cloud_free exhaustion → pause-and-ask (`QuotaExhaustedError`); cap → `BudgetExceededError`. Tier/provider/model **system-derived** (INV-7). _Schema-retry stays in the agent (ChunkingAgent pattern), not the router — see Decided._
- [x] Cost tracking per **amended** §6.6: one `llm_calls` Postgres table, one row per call **incl. refusals/failures**; record input/output **tokens whenever the provider returns them** (incl. Ollama's `eval_count`/`prompt_eval_count`), nullable `cost_estimate` (paid), nullable `gpu_seconds` (Ollama Cloud); daily / project / per-task-type aggregation read from it; per-day USD cap (`DAILY_BUDGET_USD`) **checked before dispatch** (fail-closed), bounded one-call overshoot documented.
- [x] Status endpoint surfacing budget + Ollama Cloud GPU-quota state (consumed by the M2.S5 agent activity panel). Declare non-2xx outcomes per `backend/CLAUDE.md` "API routes". **Scoped 2026-06-02 (own-review + Codex):** S2 surfaces budget/spend/remaining-USD + GPU-seconds **consumed** (from the ledger) + per-task-type breakdown. The **remaining** Ollama Cloud GPU-time *quota* (spec §6.5/§6.6 "time remaining" / "remaining session quota") needs Ollama Cloud's account API and lands with the **M2.S5** panel — accepted deferral (see Decided), consistent with ADR 0003's M2.S5 panel scope. The endpoint docstring marks the gap; no fabricated remaining-figure in the meantime.
- [x] **Deferred-egress marker:** a clear in-code note at the paid-egress point that the per-fragment consent UI is M2.S5 (D5 — no sensitive data, documented not gated).
- [x] Tests: `OpenRouterProvider` vs mocked transport (usage parsing); router decision matrix + **failover discrimination** (429 vs 401 vs 5xx **vs transport**); cost recording; cap → pause-and-ask path; end-to-end `OpenRouterProvider`→router→ledger. _**envelope-malformed vs schema-invalid** deferred to M2.S3 — the router meets a real Pydantic schema there; the malformed-`200`-envelope record/failover gap is tracked in cross-cutting._

**Done when:** a routed cloud_strong call (via `OpenRouterProvider`) against a mock returns and records a usage row; the cap path pauses-and-asks; status endpoint exposes the daily total.
**Resume anchor:** `adapters/llm/{openrouter,router}.py` exist; `base.py`/`ollama.py` carry usage; `llm_calls` table + writes; status endpoint live. (Direct vendor adapters intentionally absent.)

### Session 3 — ExtractionAgent `[x]`

_Spec §7 step 4. Cloud_free by default per §6.5 agent table; cloud_strong on hard
cases via the M2.S2 router._

> **Design settled 2026-06-08 — build directly from the accepted `architecture/proposals/m2s3-extraction-agent.md`** (register resolved; no owner-resolution step remains). Key decisions are folded into the tasks below: per-paragraph granularity (D4); single-paragraph agent, resumable batch driver → M2.S4 (D5); **`candidate_name`** surface form, *not* `canonical_name` (D1); typed `ProviderResponseError` for malformed-`200` envelopes (D2/OQ-10); soft-flag `evidence_quote` (G5); known-entities/custom-types as params now / PreNER hints deferred (D3).

- [x] `prompts/extraction.pl.j2` + `prompts/extraction.en.j2` — Appendix C.2 skeleton. **Render structure strictly from the trusted template; never reparse output rendered with user-supplied text** (encoded in `/review-pr` §4 prompt-injection-safety check; the same rule that hardened `ChunkingAgent` in Session 3).
- [x] Pydantic schema: `ExtractionProposal` with `entities: list[EntityCandidate]` + `relations: list[RelationCandidate]`; open-world types per §3.2 (string `type` field — examples constrain but no enum); validators for required fields + **non-empty `candidate_name`** (surface form per D1 — **not** `canonical_name`, which is the resolved bilingual name assigned at M3 merge); **soft-flag `evidence_quote`** (drop the quote if it isn't a whitespace-normalised substring of the paragraph, keep the candidate — G5); dangling relations accepted (M3/human resolves). _Follow-up: blank `subject`/`predicate`/`object` aren't yet rejected — see cross-cutting (external PR-#42 remark)._
- [x] `agents/extraction_agent.py` — load prompt → call **router** (`router.complete(messages, weight="medium", task_type="extraction", json_schema=…)`) → parse + validate → retry on schema violation (mirror `ChunkingAgent` retry shape, including the bias-control of giving up after N retries with a clear error). **Single-paragraph** (D5): the batch loop + pause-and-ask catcher are M2.S4; the agent propagates `Budget/QuotaExhaustedError`, never swallows them.
- [x] **Router OQ-10 (D2):** add a typed `ProviderResponseError` in `adapters/llm/base.py`, raised by adapters on a malformed-`200` envelope (missing fields, unparseable body, **and null `content`** — added in `/code-review` fold), that `router.py` records + fails over like a 5xx — distinct from a schema-invalid body (agent prompt-retry). Add the "envelope-malformed vs schema-invalid" router test.
- [x] Per-paragraph dispatch (D4) with known-entities/custom-types context per spec §7 step 4 ("Here are known entities: {existing}") **as params now** — the real Neo4j read is wired in M2.S4; first end-to-end passes empty lists. ~~**PreNER hints deferred** (parameter wired, unused until an eval — D3).~~ **As-built:** the `prener_hints` param was **dropped** (not wired-unused) per the `/code-review` fold — no speculative dead param; re-add with a concrete type when the eval lands (the D3 intent, minus the dead surface).
- [x] Tests: agent against a mocked **router**; happy path PL + EN; retry-on-malformed-JSON; schema-violation → bounded give-up; **empty-but-valid not retried**; **prompt-injection safety** — paragraphs containing `[ROLE]` markers or fake JSON can't forge structure or merge into a wrong entity. _Plus null-content envelope + grounded/ungrounded `evidence_quote` + direct `extract_json` tests added in the review fold._

**Done when:** ✅ against a mocked router, paragraph → validated entity + relation candidates; retry-on-bad-JSON proven; empty-but-valid not retried; injection-safe; `ProviderResponseError` records+fails-over. **All met; merged PR #42 (134 unit tests).**
**Resume anchor:** `agents/extraction_agent.py`, `prompts/extraction.{pl,en}.j2`, `EntityCandidate`/`RelationCandidate`/`ExtractionProposal` schemas, and `ProviderResponseError` exist.

### Session 4 — Neo4jAdapter writes (no dedupe) `[x]`

_Spec §9 M2: "Save entities to Neo4j without cascade (everything = new entity for
now)." Cascade matching (MatchingAgent, JudgeAgent, review queue — Stages 1–4) is
M3 in its entirety._

- [x] **Deps:** `/add-dependency` for the async `neo4j` Python driver. ✅ **Session 15:** `neo4j==5.28.4` (5.x LTS to match the 5.26 server; aged, OSV-clean).
- [x] `adapters/neo4j_repo.py` — async neo4j driver session helper (config from the existing M0 `.env` keys); `create_entity`, `create_relation`; node properties per §3.2 (id UUID app-side, type, canonical_name PL+EN, aliases, properties JSON, first_seen paragraph_id, embedding **nullable** — M3 fills it). ✅ **Session 15:** also `get_entity`/`count_entities`/`get_relations`/`delete_project_graph`; `CREATE`-not-`MERGE` (INV-8); open-world type backtick-escaped (Cypher-injection-safe); `properties` stored as JSON; `domain/graph.py` holds `GraphEntity`/`GraphRelation` (distinct from the agent's candidates).
- [x] Wire: ExtractionAgent output → Neo4jAdapter writes; **no Stage 1/2/3 logic** (every extracted candidate becomes a fresh node — the spec is explicit, and this exposes the duplicate problem M3 then solves). ✅ **Session 16 (PR #48):** pure `agents/extraction_graph.py` `proposal_to_graph` (provisional `canonical_name` = surface form in the project language, EN peer null; within-paragraph relation resolution, dangling dropped) + the `ExtractionCoordinator` batch driver + `POST /stories/{id}/extract`. Folded the blank `subject`/`predicate`/`object` validator (PR-#42 gap) here.
- [x] Persist `entity_mentions` in Postgres (paragraph_id ↔ entity_id back-reference per §6.4). **Write a new Alembic migration for the table** — it is *not* in M1's schema (M1 created only projects/stories/chapters/scenes/paragraphs + llm_calls; `entity_mentions` exists only in spec §6.4). Extend `EXPECTED_TABLES` in `tests/integration/test_migrations.py` to cover it. ✅ **Session 15:** migration created (`entity_id` no Postgres FK — cross-store, OQ-1); `EXPECTED_TABLES` extended; migration smoke test green. _(The repo insert fn + the write wiring are still Session 16.)_
- [ ] **Embedding read path stays deferred** — paragraphs continue to read `NULL AS embedding`. M3's MatchingAgent Stage 2 will turn it on alongside the entity-embedding writes; flag in code (don't refactor `postgres_repo` here).
- [x] Tests: integration against the neo4j compose service; round-trip read back what was written; `entity_mentions` back-reference holds; verify the no-dedupe property (two identical extractions produce two nodes). ✅ **Session 15:** round-trip + no-dedupe green vs live Neo4j. ✅ **Session 16:** the `entity_mentions` round-trip/cascade tests, the live `ExtractionCoordinator` persistence suite, the pure-mapping + batch-driver unit suites, and the route-contract suite — and the CI neo4j service makes them all **run at the gate**.
- [x] **[Session 16] Add the `neo4j` service to the backend CI job** (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) + update the `integration` marker description (now needs Neo4j too). ✅ Done (PR #48) — backend job green with neo4j+postgres services; the netty/openssl CVE-rot the neo4j scan surfaced was waived (unreachable on loopback).
- [x] **[Session 16] Map router exit exceptions → declared HTTP** on the new write path; fold the ChunkingAgent→502 cross-cutting at the same time. ✅ Done: `ProviderResponseError`/`ExtractionError`/`httpx.HTTPError` → 502; `BudgetExceeded`/`QuotaExhausted` are caught by the driver → **202-paused** (the OQ-2 + owner pause-response decision), not an HTTP error. ChunkingAgent now maps `ProviderResponseError`→`ChunkingError`→502.
- [x] **[Session 16] Resumable batch driver** (OQ-2) — the batch driver (not the agent) catches the router's pause-and-ask and resumes from the last-done graph write. ✅ Done: `ExtractionCoordinator`; checkpoint = a committed `entity_mentions` row, written **last** (after entities + relations) so a relation failure isn't falsely checkpointed (external-review fold).

**Done when:** ✅ end-to-end ingest (upload → structure → extraction → graph write) completes against a real neo4j; round-trip test green; **the integration test runs in CI** (neo4j service present). **All met; merged PR #48 (188 tests).**
**Resume anchor:** ✅ `adapters/{neo4j_repo,postgres_mention_store}.py`, `agents/{extraction_graph,extraction_coordinator}.py`, `entity_mentions` migration, `POST /stories/{id}/extract`, CI neo4j service all exist on `main`.

## Decided — Milestone 3 and earlier

_Reverse-chronological, exactly as moved from `PLAN_SHORT.md`'s Decided section._

- **2026-06-17 — Session 31 (M3→M4 roll, docs/governance — no feature code): M3 closed feature-complete; M4 opened with inline highlights decomposed; a process gap closed so review reports get acted on.** All three roll gates ran. **(1) Architecture re-sync** (`architecture/reports/2026-06-17-architecture-review.md`) — first full sweep since edges + the relation lifecycle landed (S4b–S4f); no blockers; **folded** the one decision-independent drift on sight (a ~5-session-stale `overview.md` as-built block, now "M3 feature-complete"); filed **OQ-20** (the relation lifecycle has a real status machine in code but no state-machine note — the structural gap). **(2) Cross-cutting curation M3→M4** (hand-walked per `docs/CLAUDE.md` §3) — re-titled the list, **graduated §3.4 graph story-vs-project scoping to live M4 work** (multi-story breaks the one-story-per-project assumption), added carry-forwards: DM-Rel-5 written-edge re-point (lands with M4 entity↔entity merge) + OQ-20. **(3) M4 first slice = inline highlights** (owner chose it over multi-story/§3.4 and properties-edit — foundational, low-risk, high portfolio value, unblocks side-panel + annotation). Decomposed → `architecture/proposals/m4-inline-highlights.md` (register **OPEN**, DM-IH-1..8 / OQ-21). **Key finding:** accepted `entity_mentions` carry **null char offsets**, so highlighting is a span-resolution problem (DM-IH-1), not a render of stored spans — a read-only projection (most stations n/a; INV-1/9 untouched). **(4) Retro — the report-forcing-function gap (owner-raised, both-sides change):** a review-architecture report has no forcing function (a decision register blocks the build; a waiver re-reds CI; a report's findings just sit). Closed by a **producer/consumer pairing**: new **`/resume-session` step 3c** (triage the latest report's blocker/risk findings — resolved-or-tracked — mirroring step 3b's waiver scan) ↔ **`meta-architect:review-architecture` step 7** (write findings actionable + mirror to open-questions so they're triage-able); noted in `architecture/AGENTS.md` (incl. that step 3c *reads* a report, it doesn't *run* the architect — ADR 0002 wiring stays deferred). *Considered & rejected:* record-only (the gap nearly bit this very session); a settings.json hook (heavier — resume is already mandatory). **(5) Deferred (owner):** the now-soaked **python-multipart OSV waiver drop** — fix 0.0.31 soaks 2026-06-18, couldn't drop on the 06-17 roll day (13-day-old fix fails the ≥14-day gate); drop on/after 06-18, before the 06-19 `ignoreUntil`. **Checks:** docs/vault only — code gates are no-ops; no deps changed.

- **2026-06-17 — Session 30 (M3.S4f relation-review UI, PR #78 merged): the relation human-gate UI shipped, closing M3's feature work; a frontend↔backend contract-fidelity lesson encoded both sides.** **(1) Confirm-at-build picks (owner, S30):** keyboard **A=commit / R=reject** (reuse the candidate queue's verbs for muscle memory; J/K nav) — a §8.3 *subset*, and the card shows the endpoint's **surface strings (v1)**, not resolved canonical entity names (deferred); *considered & rejected:* a `C=commit` key (diverges from the mirror) and a names lookup (extra surface this session). **No spec amendment** — §8.3 doesn't define a relations scheme and surface strings are §3.3's own wording. **(2) `/code-review` (6-finder) caught a real bug `/review-pr` missed (4th consecutive substantive PR — #36/#60/#63/#78):** `decideMessage` mapped HTTP **409 → "already decided"**, but the decide route returns 409 for a *stale/held endpoint* (`RelationEndpointsUnresolved`) and already-decided is a **200** + `already_decided:true` — and the test had *masked* it with a fabricated 409 body. Fixed the semantics + the test; folded two test gaps (`useDecideRelation` hook test mirroring `useReviewCandidate`; a graph-viewer `relations-link` assertion). **(3) Retro (2 changes, owner approved — "both homes"):** (a) *"derive an HTTP status code's meaning from the backend route, not a sibling feature's mapping; a fabricated error-body test fixture validates fiction"* → `frontend/src/lib/api/AGENTS.md` **+** `/review-pr` §2 mirror; (b) *"manual browser verification: the dev stack is long-running and `.env` is populated — migrate the dev DB first (merged migrations don't auto-apply), bring up both servers, seed fixture rows via SQL against the endpoint's real preconditions"* → `frontend/AGENTS.md`. *Considered & rejected:* skip-as-one-off for (a) (the miss was concrete and the class general — status-code mappers recur per feature) and a heavier run/verifier skill for (b) (ceremony for an occasional step). **(4) Verified-real nits left unfolded** (mirror-shared — folding here would diverge the two queues — or already tracked; see cross-cutting): keyboard A/R not gated by in-flight mutation (matches `ReviewQueue`); stale decide banner across navigation; the error-to-string mapper skeleton now **n=5**. **Reviews:** `/review-pr` (self) + `/code-review`; full frontend suite 136 green; CI 4/4 green; browser-verified end-to-end.

- **2026-06-16 — Session 29 (M3.S4e relation-write backend, PR #76 merged): graph edges now write under an explicit human gate; INV-1 broadened; a real merge-target bug fixed by `/code-review`.** Built the relation-write backend test-first, resolving the whole DM-Rel register. **(1) DM-Rel-4 = a `staged_relations` table** (owner) — a per-paragraph-occurrence row with a `staged|written|rejected` lifecycle, resolved endpoint ids, and the committed edge id; *considered & rejected:* keeping the inert JSONB blob (can't carry per-relation status/evidence for the explicit gate). Relations stage here atomically in `persist()`; `paragraph_processed.relations` is left vestigial. **(2) DM-Rel-6 edge id = `uuid5(subject_id, predicate, object_id)`** (owner) — the same fact across two paragraphs collapses to **one** edge (clean graph, §9 M3); *considered & rejected:* id-from-staged-row (preserves per-mention edges but shows two parallel edges for one fact). Owner-flagged **follow-up:** the triple-id loses per-mention provenance on the graph side → post-PoC need a way to enumerate all occurrences (the staged rows retain it). **(3) DM-Rel-2/5/7 confirmed at build as proposed:** normalised-exact same-paragraph resolution reading the committed id from `candidates`; M3 writes / M4 re-points; dangling-to-known held. The create-id derivation was **promoted to the shared `domain.candidates.committed_entity_id`** so the accept path and resolution can't drift (the DM-Rel-2 `verify-at-build` flag). **(4) Invariant: broaden INV-1** ("…and every relation edge") rather than mint INV-10 — one human-gate principle for nodes + edges; INV-9 gains its second witnessed instance. **ADR 0005** records the slice + its accepted costs; proposal → `accepted`, OQ-19 struck. **(5) No spec amendment** — §3.3 already lists "decide on relations"; the gate *mechanism* didn't force a §3.2/§3.3 change. **(6) `/code-review` caught a real bug:** when a reviewer *changes a merge target*, the candidate row's `target_entity_id` was never persisted (only the decision row was), so `committed_entity_id` resolved a same-paragraph relation endpoint to the stale target → edge to the wrong entity. *Fixed:* `set_status` now persists the committed target on merge-accept (still status-last); regression + cross-paragraph-collapse tests added. **Reviews:** `/review-pr` (self) + the 7-finder `/code-review`, both folded before merge. 331 tests pass.

- **2026-06-16 — Session 28 (planning/decompose, vault-only): relation-write framed + designed; the central gate decided; a meta-architect skill wording fixed.** No production code. **(1) Framing (owner):** the relation-write work is an **M3 slice** — relations are part of §9 M3's "the graph is clean" (and §3.3 lists "decide on relations" as a Stage-4 human action), *not* an M3→M4 milestone roll (M3's *entity* dedupe is done, S4a–S4d). So we stay in M3 and add a relation-write slice; no milestone roll. **(2) `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0** → `architecture/proposals/m3-relation-write.md` (+ glossary `referential-integrity`, OQ-19, learning-log; INDEX/changelog regenerated; the stale INDEX "Next steps" that framed S4c as next — though S4c/S4d shipped — corrected). **Key architectural finding (the reframe):** a staged relation names its endpoints as **surface strings** with no entity id until accept, so edges must be written **lazily** by resolving each endpoint to its candidate's *committed* entity id — which means the feared "re-point edges on merge" **mostly dissolves** (the edge is born pointing at the survivor; only an M4 accepted-entity↔entity merge re-points a *written* edge — DM-Rel-5). Concrete must-fix surfaced: `neo4j_repo.create_relation` uses `CREATE`, so a retried accept **doubles** the edge → needs a deterministic id + `MERGE`-on-id (DM-Rel-6). **(3) DM-Rel-1 decided (owner): an EXPLICIT human gate** over relations — the §3.3 5th action ("decide on relations"), *not* auto-write-on-both-endpoints-accepted. *Considered & rejected:* auto-write (lightest, but commits a hallucinated predicate/direction even when both nodes are right — the exact LLM error human-in-the-loop exists to catch); hybrid bulk-confirm (kept as a fallback if the explicit gate proves heavy). Implies broadening INV-1 (or minting INV-10) to put the human gate on edges — framed, decided at build. **(4) Slice (owner): split BACKEND now / UI next** (the proven S4a→S4b cut) — the backend (staged_relations table + resolution + idempotent edge + decide-relations endpoints + the invariant flip) is test-first witnessable at the API boundary; the React relation-review surface follows. *Considered & rejected:* one combined slice (too big for one conversation, the same reason S4 was split). Remaining register **DM-Rel-2/4/5/6/7 carried as proposed, confirm-at-build** (the S4a pattern). **(5) Spec consistency:** §3.3 already lists "decide on relations" as a human action, so the explicit gate is spec-faithful — **no amendment needed now** (a precise-mechanism amendment may ride the build, like S4c amended §3.3). **(6) Retro (1 change, owner ran `/retro`):** the `decompose-requirement` + `review-architecture` skills instructed "read the matching template from `templates/`", but **no `proposal.md`/`review.md` template exists** (only adr/component/state-machine/glossary-term/project + the canonical `vault-note.md`); the section structure already lives in each skill's body. Fixed the wording in both `meta-architect/skills/*/SKILL.md` to point at `vault-note.md` for frontmatter and state that proposal/review structure is the skill-body's single home. *Considered & rejected:* adding the two templates (would duplicate the skill-body section list — a second source of truth that drifts). Second finding (review-architecture-at-resume not run on this decompose-opening session) → **note-only**: fresh evidence toward OQ-3's deferred ritual-wiring, no skill change (wiring stays deferred per ADR 0002).

- **2026-06-16 — Session 27 (M3.S4d build + security treadmill): two design calls, a multi-PR security detour, and a retro skill.** **(1) Handpick ranking — no score floor.** The `GET /stories/{id}/entities?q=` search ranks with the matcher's own RapidFuzz (`search_entities` reuses a shared `_rank` that `top_alternatives` now delegates to — behaviour-preserving). The *planned* score floor was **dropped during the build** after measuring: the duplicates handpick exists to catch — "Kasia"↔"Katarzyna" (43), "Bronek"↔"Bronisław" (53) — score *below* unrelated cross-category noise ("Warszawa"↔"Wars" 67), so any floor that cuts noise also hides the target. Resolution: rank, cap at top-N, keep low matches reachable; the human (INV-1) picks. *Considered & rejected:* a floor (re-introduces the matcher's blind spot); substring/Cypher `CONTAINS` (worse for diminutives + would put `q` in Cypher). **(2) Handpick precedence — last-pick-wins.** `mergeTarget = handpicked ?? pickedAlternative` gave the handpick *static* precedence, so after handpicking you couldn't switch back to a top-3 alternative (`/code-review` caught it). Fixed: picking an alternative clears the handpick (+ its active highlight), so the most recent choice wins. **(3) Security treadmill (owner-decided approach).** On opening PR #70, CI surfaced two reds beyond the known vite #68 — a backend **OSV SCA** wave (new advisories against pinned `starlette`/`python-multipart`) and, after fixing it, an **unmasked** Trivy **neo4j** netty HIGH (CVE-2026-50010, sequential-unmask). Owner chose **soaked bumps + fix-first time-boxed waivers**: `starlette` 1.0.1→1.2.0 + `python-multipart` 0.0.27→0.0.30 + `vite` 8.0.10→8.0.16 (all soaked) clear 3 of 4 SCA HIGHs and the vite HIGH; residuals whose fixes are still in soak are waived with `ignoreUntil` + reachability (127.0.0.1 single-user, no public TLS → the DoS/MITM CVEs aren't remotely reachable) + dated drop-when (tracked in cross-cutting). Merged as PRs #72 (SCA + neo4j), #73 (vite); #68/#71 closed. *Considered & rejected:* wait ~11 days for the cleanest fixes to soak (blocks the feature); scope the pre-push age-hook (a non-security micro-opt — the local hook checks pin *age*, not CVEs; CI is the real gate). **(4) Retro — `/triage-advisory` skill + `/resume-session` step 3b.** The genuine security risk surfaced is a **forgotten waiver** (a known-vulnerable dep shipping behind a green board). New `/triage-advisory` skill owns the advisory lifecycle (enumerate gates + waivers → fix-first via `/add-dependency`/`/pin-image`, else time-boxed waiver, **and the drop-revisit** that removes a waiver when its fix lands); `/resume-session` gained a cheap **date-only waiver-expiry scan** (step 3b) so expiring waivers surface at session start, with the `ignoreUntil` CI re-red as backstop. Root `AGENTS.md` security baseline points at it. *Considered & rejected:* a settings.json SessionStart hook (heavier infra; resume is already the mandatory ritual); a new treadmill *rule* (the knowledge already lives in `/review-pr` §5/§8 + the waiver files).

- **2026-06-15 — Session 26 (M3.S4c build): ADR 0005 declined; a plain-language communication rule added.** Two non-obvious calls made during the build. **(1) ADR 0005 declined (owner).** S4c introduces the project's first *automated* writer that mutates a *staged proposal* after staging (re-match flips `new → merge` in the `candidates` table). The proposal had deferred to the owner whether that shift is ADR-worthy. Decided **no separate ADR**: it is a contained change — staging-only, never the graph, so **INV-9 holds** (its line is graph-vs-staging) and INV-1 holds (the human still commits every merge) — and the full reasoning already lives in the accepted proposal + spec §3.3. The rationale is recorded in this plan + a one-line **INV-9 graph-vs-staging clarification** in `architecture/invariants.md` + the `candidate-lifecycle` self-loop, rather than a new decision file. *Considered & rejected:* author ADR 0005 (more ceremony than a staging-only, already-documented change earns). **(2) Communication rule (retro).** Added a bullet to root `AGENTS.md` "How to communicate with me": **lead with plain language when asking the owner to decide** — state the actual tradeoff a non-specialist would follow and unpack any internal shorthand (ADR, `INV-N`, `DM-S4c-N`, slugs) rather than assuming it's shared, keeping the precise terms for the durable written record. Earned by a real correction this session (the first ADR-0005 question was too jargon-dense; the owner asked for "less lingo" — not because they're a beginner, but because dense shorthand packed together trips them up). *Considered & rejected:* treat it as a one-off (the tendency is general and owner-facing, so a durable rule fits).

- **2026-06-15 — Session 25 (M3.S4c decompose): intra-batch dedup designed; spec §3.3 amended.** The S4b browser walk made a real gap concrete — a single first-pass extraction of the sample story staged `Janek` ×3 (and `Marta`/`Konrad`/`Order` ×2) as independent NEW proposals → after accept, **duplicate Neo4j nodes the review queue could not merge**, undercutting §9 M3's "the graph is clean". The cascade only dedupes *cross-pass* (against the accepted graph at stage time); this is the *intra-batch* gap M3.S4a's own "but what if" had named and deferred. **`meta-architect:decompose-requirement`** → `architecture/proposals/m3s4c-intra-batch-rematch.md` (+ glossary `intra-batch-dedup`, OQ-18, learning-log ×2). Two additive mechanisms on S4a/S4b, **neither touching the graph** (INV-1/INV-9 *hold* — re-match is the project's first automated *staging-proposal* writer, and INV-9's line is graph-vs-staging): **(a) on-accept live re-match** (deterministic Stage 1/2 over still-pending candidates each accept → dupes flip `new → merge`; backend-only, no LLM) + **(b) manual handpick** (entity-search endpoint + picker for matcher false negatives). **Register resolved (owner):** ~~DM-S4c-1~~ split **S4c** (re-match, backend-only) + **S4d** (handpick); ~~DM-S4c-2~~ synchronous-in-accept + incremental; ~~DM-S4c-3~~ auto-flip on Stage 1 `>85%` **OR** Stage 2 `cosine >0.85` (*owner chose +Stage-2 over my proposed Stage-1-only* — catches more semantic matches; still **no live judge**), ~~DM-S4c-4~~ **monotone** (`new → merge` only) → idempotent, kept as transition guard not a new INV-10; ~~DM-S4c-5~~ handpick **project-scoped** (*considered & rejected:* cross-project/world — crosses §6.4, needs the M4 world-graph) — supersedes the deferred arbitrary-search item; ~~DM-S4c-6~~ `GET /stories/{id}/entities?q=` via `accepted_entity_reader`. *Considered & rejected:* one combined S4c+S4d session (too big); relation-write before S4d (~~deferred~~ kept deferred — but its priority rises, since merges now orphan relations). **Spec §3.3 amended** (on-accept re-match + manual-handpick clarifications + the deterministic-only cost note) via the stop-and-amend flow; vault + plan reconciled. **No code, no ADR yet** — ADR 0005 (if warranted) authors test-first with the S4c code. First S4c code = the failing re-match flip test.

- **2026-06-15 — Session 24 (M3.S4a): intercept-before-write shipped + merged (PR #63).** The M3 milestone-defining flip, test-first. **(1) The flip** — `ExtractionCoordinator` no longer writes the graph: it *stages* each candidate into a new Postgres `candidates` table with the §3.3 cascade's proposal (embed-on-extract → Matching S1/S2 → Judge S3, fail-closed), writing **zero** Neo4j nodes. The graph is written **only** by the human-accept path (`CandidateReviewService` → `POST …/candidates/{id}/accept|reject`). The flip is witnessed by the rewritten coordinator unit test + an integration test ("extract → 0 nodes, accept → 1 node"), replacing M2.S4's two-identical-→-two-nodes test. **(2) Invariants** — **INV-8 retired** (superseded by INV-1), **INV-1's first enforcer landed** (the accept handler), **INV-9 added** ("no automated stage writes the graph" — the coordinator holds no graph writer); `architecture/invariants.md` + `candidate-lifecycle.md` (→ `living`) + `overview`/`open-questions`/`glossary`/`INDEX` reconciled; **ADR 0004** authored. **(3) Design** — `create_entity` is now an idempotent MERGE-on-id (+ `add_alias` for accept-merge), so the accept path (Neo4j → mention(+vector) → evidence → **status-flip-last**) with **deterministic accept-path ids** is idempotent on a crash-before-flip retry; merge re-validates the target (TOCTOU → 409). New tables `candidates`/`candidate_decisions`/`paragraph_processed` (resume marker, fixes M2's zero-candidate reprocess wart); `PostgresCandidateStore`, `AcceptedEntityReader` (accepted-graph snapshot read once/run, the C4 mitigation). **(4) Scope** — relations are *staged* (JSONB on the marker) but the edge write + re-point-on-merge is **deferred to S4b** (a relation needs both endpoints accepted); **INV-2 consent gate deferred past M3**; §10 q8 (bilingual peering) surfaced as deferred (accept-create reuses the M2 provisional rule). Register DM-S4a-1..5 resolved. **(5) Cross-cutting folded:** store-down→503 (psycopg `OperationalError` + neo4j `ServiceUnavailable`) + a FastAPI lifespan closing the Neo4j driver. **(6) JudgeAgent hardened** (the `/code-review` catch): its give-up contract is now *total* — a terminal transport/envelope failure → `JudgeError`, so a judge outage fail-closes the candidate to the human instead of 502'ing the batch. **(7) Reviews:** `/review-pr` + multi-agent `/code-review` both ran and folded (judge fail-closed gap, idempotent re-accept `entity_id`, DM-rej docstring overclaim, dead-code removal); the GitHub Codex secondary was usage-limited (best-effort, not blocked on). 287 backend + 51 frontend tests pass; ruff/format/mypy/tsc clean; CI green 4/4; squash-merged `4c607cf`. **Retro (2 changes, approved):** (a) *"regenerating the typed API client does not reconcile its consumers — on a backend route shape change, grep `frontend/src` for the old + new field names"* → `frontend/src/lib/api/AGENTS.md` + `/review-pr` §2 (a renamed `ExtractResponse` field left 3 frontend test fixtures red in CI, not review); (b) *"make an agent's give-up error total (wrap transport/envelope → give-up) so a consumer can fail-close on one exception type"* → `backend/src/story_forge/AGENTS.md` (Agents) + `/review-pr` §1. *Considered & rejected:* note-only for both (each miss was concrete and the class is general). **Vault derived notes** (INDEX priority queue item 13) flagged for the next `meta-architect:review-architecture` re-sync.

- **2026-06-15 — Session 22 (M3.S3): Stage 3 `JudgeAgent` (LLM-as-judge) shipped + merged (PR #60), proposal-only; DM5 resolved; rule-of-three folded; §3.3 amended.** Test-first. **(1) JudgeAgent** — router-wired like `ExtractionAgent` (`complete(weight="medium", task_type="judge")` → cloud_free per §6.5); strict §3.3 verdict schema `{match: bool, confidence: float∈[0,1], reasoning: non-empty str}` (a parseable-but-degenerate body — out-of-range confidence, blank reasoning — **fails and retries**, never passes); `classify_verdict` proposes a merge **iff `match AND confidence > 0.8`** (strict edge mirrors Stage 1/2; **fail-closed — a confident NO never auto-merges**). Proposal-only/**unwired** — INV-8 still live; the cascade coordinator that maps a `JudgeError` give-up to "uncertain → review queue" lands M3.S4. **(2) DM5 resolved** — judge tier = cloud_free via `weight="medium"`/`task_type="judge"` (spec §6.5-settled; *confirmed*, not re-decided). **(3) §3.3 amended** (stop-and-amend, owner-approved): a Stage-3 merge-rule clarification — `confidence` is the judge's certainty the two are the *same*, so merge needs `match=true AND confidence > 0.8`; the box's "confidence > 0.8 → merge" is the confident-yes shorthand; the cascade stays fail-closed (no automated stage commits). **(4) Prompt fidelity — the multi-agent `/code-review` catch:** the prompt was first built from §3.3 *prose* and silently dropped **Appendix C.3**'s existing-entity `aliases` (the diminutive signal Stage 3 exists to use) + candidate `type`/`properties`; the single `/review-pr` missed it, `/code-review` caught it; folded to match C.3 in full (both PL/EN), with tests asserting every field reaches the model. `match_stage3_confidence` (default 0.8) joined `config.py` **with its reader** (no dead config). **(5) Rule-of-three fold:** `agents/validation.py` `validate_with_retry` — the shared `render → call → validate → retry-on-ValidationError → give-up` loop; `ChunkingAgent` + `ExtractionAgent` refactored onto it (each keeps its own schema/call/error). `TaskWeight` + a `Router` Protocol promoted into `adapters/llm/base.py` from `extraction_agent`'s local mirror. - **2026-06-10 — Session 16: M2.S4 completed + merged (PR #48); OQ-1/OQ-2 resolved; CVE-rot waived across 3 images; 2 retro rules.** The wiring half, test-first, squash-merged green. **(1) OQ-1 (two-store write consistency) — option (c):** write **Neo4j-then-Postgres** and **accept eventual inconsistency** at PoC (single user, reversible); no reconciliation/outbox. *Rejected:* a startup repair sweep (code for a rare local-crash window) and an outbox (over-engineered for the PoC). **(2) OQ-2 (resumable ingest) — option (a):** the **batch driver** (`ExtractionCoordinator`), not the agent, owns the budget/quota pause-and-ask; the single-paragraph agent keeps *propagating* it (M2.S3 D5). Pre-existing infra rot, not M2.S4 code; Issue #22 treadmill. **(7) Retro (2 rules, both approved):** `/review-pr` gained a **checkpoint/resume-marker ordering** check (a marker written mid-sequence lets a later step fail over a "done" record — enumerate *each* inter-write window; the P1 bug *both* my review passes missed and external review caught) and a **multi-range CVE-advisory** check (confirm which of an advisory's several vulnerable ranges your version falls in). *Considered & rejected:* note-only (both trace to concrete this-session misses and generalize).
- **2026-06-09 — Session 15: M2.S4 foundation built (unmerged branch); two latent infra bugs found by running it; 4 retro changes.** A build session; the foundation is on `feat/m2s4-neo4j-writes`, **not merged** (half-feature + the integration test would be dead at the CI gate without a Neo4j service — merging it would read as "covered" when it isn't). **(1) Driver: `neo4j==5.28.4`** — the **5.x LTS** driver line to match the 5.26-community server (same-major = lowest compatibility risk). *Rejected:* the newer 6.x line (targets the 2025.x servers we don't run). **(2) Graph modelling:** `domain/graph.py` `GraphEntity`/`GraphRelation` are the *persisted* shapes, **distinct from the agent's `*Candidate`** (candidate has a surface `candidate_name`, no id/canonical/embedding — the M2→M3 boundary). The adapter uses **`CREATE`, never `MERGE`** (the load-bearing keyword for INV-8 no-dedupe — a `MERGE`-on-name would silently violate it); the open-world relation `type` is **backtick-escaped** when interpolated (Cypher-injection-safe — the analogue of prompt-injection hardening, since the type is LLM-produced); `properties` is stored as a **JSON string** (Neo4j can't hold a nested map), `aliases` as a native list. *Rejected:* a global `MATCH (n) DETACH DELETE n` test cleanup (unsafe on a shared instance) → per-test `project_id` scoping instead. **(3) `entity_mentions` migration:** `paragraph_id` is a real FK (cascades with the tree);
