**DM7 → INV-2 consent gate deferred past M3** (persona-justified; its fourth re-point replaced by an explicit dated deferral); **DM-rej → remember rejections** (a `candidate_decisions` evidence row the matcher consults); and the S4a build register **DM-S4a-1..5** — a new `candidates` staging table, a new **INV-9** ("no automated stage writes the graph"), a staged-candidates resume checkpoint (mentions move to accept-time), a focused `candidate_decisions` evidence table now (deferring §4.2's full `edit_history` to the editing milestone), and no retention at PoC. **Checks:** no code touched (green-state code gates N/A); the vault + plan are the deliverables; the wrap is the only commit. **Retro:** nothing earned a skill/rule change; the one data-point — *run `review-architecture` at resume, not wrap, when a session opens with a decompose* — was folded into the vault's ritual-wiring evidence note. **Lesson:** at a branchy milestone-closing boundary, spending a whole conversation on the drift sweep + decompose + decisions (and *not* code) is the cheap way to keep the heavy build test-first and `main` never half-flipped — the re-slice and the five build-detail decisions would otherwise have surfaced mid-implementation, the most expensive place to discover them.
- **2026-06-15 — Session 22: M3.S3 shipped — `JudgeAgent` Stage 3 (LLM-as-judge), test-first, squash-merged green (PR #60).** The cascade's Stage-3 rung: an LLM judge that, for a candidate Stages 1–2 left *ambiguous*, returns a strict verdict `{match, confidence, reasoning}` and routes it to a merge proposal or "new/uncertain". Router-wired like `ExtractionAgent` (`weight="medium"`/`task_type="judge"` → cloud_free, **DM5 resolved**); the schema is strict (a degenerate body — out-of-range confidence, blank reasoning — fails and retries); `classify_verdict` merges only on a confident *yes* (`match AND confidence > 0.8`, strict, fail-closed — a confident *no* never auto-merges). The prompt follows spec **Appendix C.3** in full (PL + EN), injection-safe. **Proposal-only/unwired** — INV-8 is still the live no-dedupe contract until M3.S4, so nothing reaches the graph. Carried the **rule-of-three fold**: the per-agent retry loop became `agents/validation.py` `validate_with_retry`, with Chunking + Extraction refactored onto it, and `TaskWeight` + a `Router` Protocol promoted into `adapters/llm/base.py`. **Reviews — the layered gate earned its keep again:** `/review-pr` (primary) passed, but the multi-agent **`/code-review` caught a real spec-fidelity gap the single pass missed** — the prompt, built from §3.3 *prose*, had dropped Appendix C.3's existing-entity `aliases` (the diminutive signal Stage 3 exists for) + candidate `type`/`properties`; folded to match C.3 before merge. The GitHub Codex secondary reviewer was usage-limited (didn't run) — best-effort, not blocked on. **Spec §3.3 amended** (stop-and-amend, owner-approved) with the Stage-3 merge-rule clarification. **Checks:** 202 unit tests pass, ruff+format+mypy clean, CI green 4/4. **Retro (1 change):** encoded *"build an agent prompt from the spec's Appendix C template, not the §3 prose alone"* into `backend/src/story_forge/AGENTS.md` + `/review-pr` §2 — a building-time guard so the C.3-omission class is prevented at authoring, not only caught at review. **Lessons:** (a) the spec specifies each agent's prompt in *two* homes — §3 prose and the authoritative Appendix C template — and building from the prose alone silently drops fields; (b) with the secondary reviewer unavailable, the multi-agent `/code-review` is the safety net that catches what one self-review can't — direct evidence the "run `/code-review` for substantive code" rule pays for itself.
- **2026-06-12 — Session 21: M3.S2 shipped — `MatchingAgent` Stage 2 (embedding cosine) + the pgvector foundation, test-first, squash-merged green (PR #58).** Built Stage 2 and the whole pgvector persistence under it, **foundation-only**: the embedding stack is built + tested but stays out of the live extraction path until the cascade is wired (M3.S4) — mentions are recorded with `embedding=None`, mirroring the spaCy/PreNER built-but-unwired precedent and honouring INV-8 (no behaviour change yet). The mid-session call (foundation-only vs wire-now-with-graceful-degradation) was surfaced as a `/plan`-mode question and decided with the owner before any code. **Shipped:** `pgvector==0.4.2` (core) + an optional `embeddings` group (`sentence-transformers`/`torch`/`transformers`/`huggingface-hub`, ~2 GB, CI-skippable); a scoped **torch OSV waiver** (`GHSA-rrmf-rvhw-rf47`, MEDIUM, `torch.jit.script` unreachable, no fix); the §6.7 HF-model pin (`paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2`, 768-dim, by commit SHA via `scripts/pin_hf_model.py`, verified-at-build on CPU); an `entity_mentions.embedding vector(768)` migration; `register_vector_async` centralised in a new `db.connect` helper across all three connect sites; the paragraph reads un-stubbed from `NULL AS embedding` to the real column; and `MatchingAgent.stage2` (max cosine, strict `>0.85`, `match_stage2_cosine_merge` in config), proposal-only/unwired. **Reviews:** `/review-pr` caught a flawed `stage2` sentinel (`-1.0` → `float("-inf")`; + regression test); `/code-review` caught a `db.connect` connection leak on the registration-failure path. Both folded before merge. **Checks:** 231 unit+integration pass (incl. 2 new pgvector round-trip tests), ruff+mypy clean, dep-age + OSV green, full CI green. **Retro:** generalised the `backend/AGENTS.md` detect-secrets note to cover any high-entropy hex literal (the pinned model SHA tripped it, where before only Alembic ids were documented). **Lessons:** (a) when a step bundles a behaviour change (here, wiring a heavy optional dep into the live path) under foundation work, *surface it as an explicit scope question* — `/plan` + AskUserQuestion caught it before code, exactly where the cost is lowest. (b) a handoff that hardcodes an infra id (`down_revision`) drifts when later work moves the head — verify against `alembic heads` at write time, don't trust the literal.

This **retires the temporary INV-8** rather than layering on it, and lands **INV-1's** first enforcer; cost accepted = M2.S4's CREATE-on-extract path is refactored and the graph is empty until review. *Rejected (B) write-then-dedupe* (a dirty graph until review contradicts INV-1). **ADR 0004 + the INV-8→INV-1 fold in `invariants.md` + finalising the candidate-lifecycle note are deferred to the M3-code session, test-first** — the invariant flip is witnessed by the failing test, not asserted ahead of it. Register items DM1–DM5, DM7, DM-rej stay OPEN. **Checks:** docs/vault only — no backend/frontend code touched, so the code gates are no-ops; pre-commit (detect-secrets, whitespace, EOF) passed. **Retro: no skill/CLAUDE.md changes** — the rituals served well (the `review-architecture` sweep caught the INV-2 consent-gate drift the plan alone would have missed; the decompose framed DM6 cleanly); the only friction was cosmetic (very long single-tool writes read as stalls — a working-style note, not a rule). **Lessons:** (a) a deferral with a *named landing milestone* rots into silent drift the moment that milestone passes unmet — a milestone-boundary `review-architecture` sweep is what catches the slip (INV-2's lapsed M2.S5 target). (b) an invariant can be *vacuously* satisfied (INV-6 "keys never logged" holds only because nothing logs) — name the vacuity so it's re-examined when the precondition arrives. (c) the milestone roll is the right moment to draw the first state machine — the candidate lifecycle becomes live code in M3, and DM6 (gate-the-write) is exactly the kind of branchy call a step-0 decompose exists to surface before code.

(b) a convention file (`AGENTS.md`) stating an unimplemented capability in present tense is real portfolio drift a stranger would believe — but it lives outside any diff, so it's caught by working-nearby or a periodic sweep, not PR review.

`backend/AGENTS.md` got a **collation-mismatch** troubleshooting note (host-glibc upgrade blocks the local integration tier); `frontend/AGENTS.md` got a **smoke-walk CORS/port note** (Vite→5174 falls outside the §6.7 allowlist); `frontend/src/AGENTS.md` got a **test-first-for-React nuance** (strict for logic/hooks; presentational components shaped-then-tested, every behaviour covered + untestable surface isolated). **Lessons:** (a) an absolute quantifier in a spec amendment is exactly where as-built drift (a nullable field, an early return) hides — grep the exception path before writing "always". (b) "PR green, main red" is usually an infra flake (registry pull timeout) on a job that does external I/O — diagnose + re-run, don't assume a regression. (c) isolating the one jsdom-untestable surface (`GraphCanvas`) keeps the rest unit-testable and the browser-smoke scope tiny.

smoke-run it. (d) wrapping mid-feature (foundation green, unmerged) is a legitimate, explicitly-agreed exception to the merge-then-wrap order.
- **2026-06-08 — Session 14: backend SCA gate built + merged (PR #44); client DevSecOps notes folded into PLAN_LONG; one retro change.** Built the accepted `backend-dependency-advisory-scan` proposal on one branch, test-first (the gate's own red→green self-test). **(build)** New `osv-scanner` step in the CI `security` job scans `backend/uv.lock` **fail-on-any**; scanner pinned by **immutable image digest** (`ghcr.io/google/osv-scanner@sha256:64e8…`, v2.3.8) — *not* a GitHub Action: `google/osv-scanner-action`'s root `action.yml` is a no-`runs:` stub and its reusable workflows do diff/SARIF scans, neither a scoped fail-on-any step; a digest pin is stronger than the proposal's planned SHA-pin (D6 intent preserved, mechanism changed). - **2026-06-02 — Session 11 complete: M2.S2 built — paid LLM tier + router + cost ledger (PR #36, squash `919f9ce`).** First product code on the M2.S2 decisions (ADR 0003). (b) recording a *failure* must outlive the request that fails — the cost store commits on its own connection. (c) `detect-secrets` foot-guns (keyword-in-var-name, alembic hex ids) are now documented so the next migration/adapter-test doesn't re-discover them.

(b) a "test that runs only in CI when a 950 MB model is present" is no CI test at all; factoring a pure seam restored coverage. (c) gating on the right timestamp matters — tag-publish ≠ asset-upload, and uv locks the asset. (c) running the audit in the same wrap commit *while the Codex catch was fresh* was the user's call and the right one; deferring would have left lingering doubt.

No code touched; no green-state gates to re-run. **Lesson:** an inherited handoff's "likely shape" parenthetical is guidance, not gospel — verify each bullet against the spec before encoding it as the new slice. Retro skipped by choice (no friction surfaced; the drift catch is already a process win recorded in Decided).

- **2026-05-26 — Session 6 complete: frontend upload + outline editor — M1 closed (PR #18, squash `ee1834f`; bundled with PR #19 pgvector waiver wave 2, squash `e207ed7`, that landed mid-session).** Shipped the M1 browser-side flow end to end: upload a `.txt`/`.md`/`.docx`, see the detected language + paragraph count, continue to a manual-mode outline editor seeded with the uploaded source via router state, edit `##`/`###` markers with a live preview (TS mirror of the backend's `domain/chunking.parse_manual_outline`), submit, see persisted chapter/scene/paragraph counts. **Frontend:** `src/lib/api/client.ts` (typed fetch helpers + `ApiError(status, detail, body)` for status-discriminated UX), `useUploadStory` / `useStructureStory` hooks, `UploadScreen` (picker + drag-drop + 415/413/400-specific error copy + "Continue to outline →" Link carrying `rawText` via router state), `OutlineEditor` (mode picker, manual/hybrid textarea + live preview, 404/409/422/502-specific error copy, empty-editor-disabled-submit guard with inline hint, post-success disabled + "Outline built ✓" relabel), `outlineParse` (TS mirror parser with 6 unit tests pinning the rules), `cn()` helper at canonical `src/lib/utils.ts` (shadcn-shaped, ready for first hand-vendored primitive), `e2e.test.tsx` at `src/test/` walking the full M1 flow under jsdom. `Landing.tsx` removed; `/` now hosts `UploadScreen`. **Backend (Option B):** `StoryUploadResponse` echoes `raw_text` so the editor opens pre-seeded; `POST /stories/{id}/structure` accepts optional `{raw_text?}` body that overrides + persists in the same transaction via new `update_story_raw_text` repo helper (lock window stays small — override write post-lock). **Tests:** 29 frontend (4 hook + 3 upload + 6 editor + 6 parser + 1 e2e + 1 shell + 2 hook defense-in-depth) + 75 backend (+2 new: raw_text in upload response, manual override-and-persist); all gates clean (ruff/format/mypy --strict 21 src files; eslint/prettier/tsc/vite-build/dep-age). All four CI jobs green pre-merge. **Review:** `/review-pr` (run *before* Codex per the Session 4 bias-control) caught one destructive bug (empty-`raw_text` overwrite — Should-fix #1) and three smaller items (dead `postJson` helper, post-success UX, e2e test location). Caught the CORS 127.0.0.1 issue and the unmigrated-dev-DB gap — both folded in this wrap commit. **Lessons:** (a) the bias-controlled order (`/review-pr` *before* Codex) keeps working — Codex caught the same bug class I did but with a different mechanism; the win was *folding both*, not picking. (b) real-browser smoke-testing catches an entire class CI can't (response visible-to-JS vs server-returned). (c) one-conversation sessions can stretch across layers (frontend session → backend route extension) when surfaced explicitly via `AskUserQuestion`.

- **2026-05-25 — Session 4 complete: chunking modes + outline persistence (PR #13, squash `ceb832d`).** Shipped the §3.1 three-mode dispatch and the §7 step-2 endpoint. `domain/chunking.py` — pure `parse_manual_outline` on heading *levels* (`##` chapter, `###` scene, `#` story-title dropped; preamble + scene-before-chapter land in implicit untitled nodes so no text is lost) + `outline_to_tree` (assigns `order_index` and threads FK ids chapter→scene→paragraph; covered by direct unit tests). `agents/chunking_coordinator.py` — three-mode dispatch over an `OutlineProposer` `Protocol` (`ChunkingAgent` satisfies it structurally, tests need no `# type: ignore`); hybrid fills only untitled *scenes* so every explicit `##`/`###` survives — including a `### Cold Open` before any `##`. `proposal_to_outline` enforces the end-index-vs-count upper bound (closes Session 3 carry-forward). `ChunkingTooLongError` guards LLM paths above `max_input_words` (windowing-deferred). `POST /stories/{id}/structure?mode=auto|manual|hybrid` — one-shot build+persist; 404/409/422/502 mapped; the DB write lock (`SELECT ... - **2026-05-21 — Issue #4 closed: both CVE-stale images fixed, `main` fully green (infra/governance, no M1 code).** pgvector `0.8.1-pg17-bookworm` → `0.8.2-pg17-trixie` (the pre-approved 7-day-rule bend for a CVE-fix release; trixie carries 9 OS CVEs vs bookworm's 13, and older is strictly worse — 0.8.1-trixie = 42). Fixing it unmasked a second stale image, ollama `0.22.1` (sequential-Trivy masking, the same pattern neo4j→pgvector showed in #2) → bumped to `0.24.0` (freshest aged stable, 7 days, no bend; dropped the CRITICAL + 6 others, 17 → 12 HIGH). Residual CVEs that no tag can fix are waived per-CVE in scoped `infra/trivy/{pgvector,ollama}.trivyignore` — pgvector's OS CVEs (no fresher rebuild) + bundled `gosu`/Go-stdlib, and ollama's compiled-in Go-stdlib + `buger/jsonparser` — each with a reachability assessment (none network-reachable on a 127.0.0.1 single-user non-root deployment: gnutls unused since Postgres TLS is OpenSSL, no DTLS, no systemd daemon; ollama CVEs are mostly DoS a trusted local caller self-inflicts, the two cert-validation ones need MITM of outbound TLS). Added `infra/trivy/WAIVERS.md`, a consolidated review register (every waived CVE across neo4j/pgvector/ollama with fixed-in versions + drop conditions) for periodic re-checking. Applied to `docker-compose.yml`, the CI backend `postgres` service container, the wrapper `infra/ollama/Dockerfile`, and both Trivy scan steps. pgvector waiver verified locally (dockerized Trivy → exit 0); ollama CVE list enumerated from the CI Trivy run. Squash-merged (PR #6, `4cb92a2`), Issue #4 closed. **Process (retro):** amended `/pin-image` — local-Trivy-unreadable → push-and-harvest-from-CI fallback; scan all images up front; record waivers in `WAIVERS.md`. **Lesson:** the sequential-Trivy unmask is now a confirmed *pattern*, not a one-off — fixing image N reveals staleness in image N+1, so sweep every image the security job scans before declaring it will go green. And in this environment local Trivy on large images is unusable (sandboxed background), so CI is the authoritative scanner.
